	(function () {
		function genUID() {
			return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
				var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
				return v.toString(16);
			});
		}

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			var cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');

			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		var expireDate = new Date(),
			beacon = getCookieValue('wikia_beacon_id'),
			sessionId = getCookieValue('tracking_session_id'),
			pvNumber = getCookieValue('pv_number'),
			pvNumberGlobal = getCookieValue('pv_number_global');

		if (beacon) {
			window.beacon_id = beacon;
		}

		window.sessionId = sessionId ? sessionId : genUID();
		window.pvNumber = pvNumber ? parseInt(pvNumber, 10) + 1 : 1;
		window.pvNumberGlobal = pvNumberGlobal ? parseInt(pvNumberGlobal, 10) + 1 : 1;
		window.pvUID = genUID();

		expireDate = new Date(expireDate.getTime() + 1000 * 60 * 30);
		document.cookie = 'tracking_session_id=' + window.sessionId + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
			';domain=' + window.wgCookieDomain + '; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';
		document.cookie = 'pv_number=' + window.pvNumber + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
			'; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';
		document.cookie = 'pv_number_global=' + window.pvNumberGlobal + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
			';domain=' + window.wgCookieDomain + '; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';
	})();

	trackingOptIn.pushToUserConsentQueue(function (optIn) {
		adsApi.isNetzathletenEnabled()
			.then(function(isServiceEnabled) {
				// user opt-ins for NetzAthleten
				if (optIn && isServiceEnabled) {
					loadNetzAthletenScript();
				}
			});
	});
});
</script>
<!-- End NetzAthleten (Netletix) Tag -->

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="Actor">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Portrayed by</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Kit_Harington" title="Kit Harington">Kit Harington</a></div>
</div>
</aside>

<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:The Last of the Starks">"<i>You've got the North in you - the <u>real</u> North.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8213;<a href="/wiki/Tormund" title="Tormund">Tormund</a><span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/The_Last_of_the_Starks" title="The Last of the Starks">[src]</a></sup></span></div>
</dd></dl>
<p><b>Jon Snow</b>, born <b>Aegon Targaryen</b>, is the son of <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna Stark</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rhaegar_Targaryen" title="Rhaegar Targaryen">Rhaegar Targaryen</a>, the late <a href="/wiki/Prince_of_Dragonstone" title="Prince of Dragonstone">Prince of Dragonstone</a>. From infancy, Jon is presented as the <a href="/wiki/Bastardy" title="Bastardy">bastard</a> son of <a href="/wiki/Lord_of_Winterfell" title="Lord of Winterfell">Lord</a> <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a>, Lyanna's brother, and raised alongside his lawful children at <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a>, the seat of <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">House Stark</a>. However, his true parentage is kept secret from everyone, including Jon himself, in order to protect him from those that sought the complete annihilation of <a href="/wiki/House_Targaryen" title="House Targaryen">House Targaryen</a> after <a href="/wiki/Robert%27s_Rebellion" title="Robert's Rebellion">Robert's Rebellion</a> and to maintain order in the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Kingdoms" title="Seven Kingdoms">realm</a>.
</p><p>In order to escape his bastard status, Jon joins the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night's Watch">Night's Watch</a> and is eventually chosen as <a href="/wiki/Lord_Commander_of_the_Night%27s_Watch" title="Lord Commander of the Night's Watch">Lord Commander</a>. However, he is later murdered in a <a href="/wiki/Mutiny_at_Castle_Black" title="Mutiny at Castle Black">mutiny</a> due to his sympathy for the <a href="/wiki/Free_Folk" title="Free Folk">Free Folk</a>. Using the power of <a href="/wiki/R%27hllor" title="R'hllor">R'hllor</a>, Jon is resurrected by the <a href="/wiki/Red_Priest" title="Red Priest">Red Priestess</a> <a href="/wiki/Melisandre" title="Melisandre">Melisandre</a> at the behest of <a href="/wiki/Knighthood" title="Knighthood">Ser</a> <a href="/wiki/Davos_Seaworth" title="Davos Seaworth">Davos Seaworth</a>. Freed from his Night's Watch vows, Jon joins his "half-sister," <a href="/wiki/Sansa_Stark" title="Sansa Stark">Sansa Stark</a>, in building an army and together they retake <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a> from <a href="/wiki/House_Bolton" title="House Bolton">House Bolton</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Bastards" title="Battle of the Bastards">Battle of the Bastards</a>, restoring House Stark's dominion over <a href="/wiki/The_North" title="The North">the North</a>. Following the execution of <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_Bolton" title="Ramsay Bolton">Ramsay Bolton</a>, Jon is declared <a href="/wiki/King_in_the_North" title="King in the North">King in the North</a>.
</p><p>When the<a href="/wiki/Daenerys_Targaryen%27s_war_for_Westeros" title="Daenerys Targaryen's war for Westeros"> war for Westeros</a> begins, Jon negotiates with <a href="/wiki/Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Daenerys Targaryen">Daenerys Targaryen</a>, Rhaegar's sister, to secure her support against the <a href="/wiki/White_Walkers" title="White Walkers">White Walkers</a>, her <a href="/wiki/Dragons" title="Dragons">dragons</a> and abundance of <a href="/wiki/Dragonglass" title="Dragonglass">obsidian</a> on her military base of <a href="/wiki/Dragonstone_(island)" title="Dragonstone (island)">Dragonstone</a> providing a distinct advantage in the <a href="/wiki/Great_War" title="Great War">Great War</a>. After successfully <a href="/wiki/Wight_Hunt" title="Wight Hunt">capturing</a> a <a href="/wiki/Captured_wight" title="Captured wight">wight</a> and <a href="/wiki/Dragonpit_Summit" title="Dragonpit Summit">presenting</a> it to <a href="/wiki/King_of_the_Andals,_the_Rhoynar,_and_the_First_Men" title="King of the Andals, the Rhoynar, and the First Men">Queen</a> <a href="/wiki/Cersei_Lannister" title="Cersei Lannister">Cersei Lannister</a> as proof that the <a href="/wiki/Wights" title="Wights">army of the dead</a> is real, Jon pledges himself and his army to Daenerys, whom he falls in love with, subsequently abdicating and being named <a href="/wiki/Warden" title="Warden">Warden of the North</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon returns to Winterfell with Daenerys and the Targaryen forces, reuniting with his "half-siblings" <a href="/wiki/Arya_Stark" title="Arya Stark">Arya</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bran_Stark" title="Bran Stark">Bran Stark</a>, who discovers his true parentage. After his lineage is revealed to him by <a href="/wiki/Samwell_Tarly" title="Samwell Tarly">Samwell Tarly</a>, he fights in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Winterfell_(Great_War)" title="Battle of Winterfell (Great War)">Battle of Winterfell</a>, during which the <a href="/wiki/Night_King" title="Night King">Night King</a> is defeated and the return of the <a href="/wiki/Long_Night" title="Long Night">Long Night</a> is prevented. Afterwards, Jon aids Daenerys in her resumed campaign to take the <a href="/wiki/Iron_Throne" title="Iron Throne">Iron Throne</a> and participates in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Battle of King's Landing">Battle of King's Landing</a>. However, when Daenerys lays waste to a surrendered <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Landing" title="King's Landing">King's Landing</a>, Jon attempts, but fails, to prevent his <a href="/wiki/Man-at-arms" title="Man-at-arms">men</a> from sacking the city. Unable to dissuade Daenerys from this path, a conflicted Jon <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Assassination of Daenerys Targaryen">assassinates</a> her to prevent further carnage, and is taken prisoner by the <a href="/wiki/Unsullied" title="Unsullied">Unsullied</a>. Following the <a href="/wiki/Great_Council_of_305_AC" title="Great Council of 305 AC">Great Council of 305 AC</a>, Bran, who is elected as King of the Six Kingdoms, negotiates with the Targaryen allies, and Jon is ultimately sent into <a href="/wiki/Exile" title="Exile">exile</a> as a compromise, returning to the Night's Watch for <a href="/wiki/Regicide" title="Regicide">regicide</a>.
</p><p>After returning to Castle Black, he reunites with his <a href="/wiki/Direwolves" title="Direwolves">direwolf</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">Ghost</a>, after which he leads the remaining Free Folk to settle in the thawing <a href="/wiki/Beyond_the_Wall" title="Beyond the Wall">free lands</a>.
</p>
<nav id="toc" class="toc" data-loaded="false"><div id="toctitle"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctoggle">[<a href="#" class="internal" id="togglelink" data-show="show" data-hide="hide">show</a>]</span></div><ol></ol></nav>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Secret_origin">Secret origin</span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:The Winds of Winter">"<i>His name is [...] If Robert finds out, he'll kill him. You know he will. You have to protect him. Promise me, Ned. Promise me.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8213;Lyanna Stark to her brother Ned, speaking of her son Jon Snow.<span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/The_Winds_of_Winter" title="The Winds of <figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/19/Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20160704072306" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg" 	data-image-name="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/19/Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160704072306"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/19/Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160704072306" 	 alt="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg" 	data-image-name="Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Game-of-Thrones-S6-Ep10-The-Winds-of-Winter-Baby-Jon-Snow.jpeg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon Snow as an infant.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Eighteen years before the <a href="/wiki/War_of_the_Five_Kings" title="War of the Five Kings">War of the Five Kings</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rhaegar_Targaryen" title="Rhaegar Targaryen">Rhaegar Targaryen</a> allegedly <a href="/wiki/Abduction_of_Lyanna_Stark" title="Abduction of Lyanna Stark">abducted</a> <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna Stark</a> of <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a> in a scandal that would lead to the outbreak of <a href="/wiki/Robert%27s_Rebellion" title="Robert's Rebellion">Robert's Rebellion</a>. Rhaegar would eventually return to fight in the war, but not before leaving Lyanna behind at the <a href="/wiki/Tower_of_Joy" title="Tower of Joy">Tower of Joy</a>, guarded by <a href="/wiki/Lord_Commander_of_the_Kingsguard" title="Lord Commander of the Kingsguard">Lord Commander</a> <a href="/wiki/Gerold_Hightower" title="Gerold Hightower">Gerold Hightower</a> and Ser <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Dayne" title="Arthur Dayne">Arthur Dayne</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Kingsguard" title="Kingsguard">Kingsguard</a>. Lord <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a>, Lyanna's brother, rode to war along with her betrothed, <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">Robert Baratheon</a>, to rescue his sister and avenge the <a href="/wiki/Execution_of_Rickard_and_Brandon_Stark" title="Execution of Rickard and Brandon Stark">deaths</a> of their <a href="/wiki/Rickard_Stark" title="Rickard Stark">father</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brandon_Stark_(son_of_Rickard)" title="Brandon Stark (son of Rickard)">brother</a> on the orders of Rhaegar's father, <a href="/wiki/Aerys_II_Targaryen" title="Aerys II Targaryen">Aerys II</a>, the Mad King.
</p><p>Robert would ultimately kill Rhaegar at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Trident" title="Battle of the Trident">Battle of the Trident</a>, effectively ensuring their victory in the war. After the <a href="/wiki/Sack_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Sack of King's Landing">Sack of King's Landing</a>, Ned continued south in search of his sister and ultimately found her at the Tower of Joy in the <a href="/wiki/Red_Mountains" title="Red Mountains">Red Mountains</a> at the border of Dorne. Ned and his companions engaged in a <a href="/wiki/Showdown_at_the_Tower_of_Joy" title="Showdown at the Tower of Joy">final fierce melee</a> with the remaining Targaryen Kingsguard, which resulted in the deaths of all combatants save Ned himself and <a href="/wiki/Howland_Reed" title="Howland Reed">Howland Reed</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E53_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E53-2">[3]</a></sup>
</p><p>After defeating the last of the Kingsguard, Ned rushed into the tower to save his sister - only to find Lyanna dying from <i>childbirth</i>, having just given birth to Rhaegar's own son. Desperate to protect the life of her newborn child, a fading Lyanna pleaded with Ned to promise her that he would keep her son safe, and his true heritage hidden from Robert as he had been Rhaegar's most bitter enemy. Furthermore, the boy's existence was a potential threat to Robert's claim to the <a href="/wiki/Iron_Throne" title="Iron Throne">Iron Throne</a> after the deaths of Rhaegar's other children, <a href="/wiki/Rhaenys_Targaryen_(daughter_of_Rhaegar)" title="Rhaenys Targaryen (daughter of Rhaegar)">Rhaenys</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aegon_Targaryen_(son_of_Rhaegar)" title="Aegon Targaryen (son of Rhaegar)" class="mw-redirect">Aegon</a>, by his wife <a href="/wiki/Elia_Martell" title="Elia Martell">Elia Martell</a>, who also perished, during the Sack of King's Landing. In accordance with her last wish, Ned resolved to pass Lyanna's son off as his own <a href="/wiki/Bastardy" title="Bastardy">bastard</a>and raise him in his home castle - a great blow to his honor as he knew that his decision would shame both himself and his lady wife, <a href="/wiki/Catelyn_Tully" title="Catelyn Tully" class="mw-redirect">Catelyn Tully</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E60_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E60-3">[4]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[5]</a></sup>
</p><p>Ned decided not to use his nephew's birth name of Aegon, which would have given away his real parentage. Instead, he chose to give the baby the name "Jon" after his great friend and mentor <a href="/wiki/Jon_Arryn" title="Jon Arryn">Jon Arryn</a>, Lord of the Vale, whom he loved like a second father. The boy also grew up using the surname "Snow", as is customary for acknowledged bastards in the <a href="/wiki/The_North" title="The North">North</a>. In truth, however, "Jon" is not a bastard at all, as Rhaegar apparently had his marriage to Elia annulled and married Lyanna.<sup id="cite_ref-E65_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E65-5">[6]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h3>
<p>Jon Snow spent the next seventeen years being raised in Winterfell as Lord Eddard's illegitimate son, alongside his trueborn children with his wife. Understandably, Eddard never told anyone, including Catelyn or Jon himself, who his mother was or even if she was still alive. When pressed by King Robert Baratheon, whom he couldn't deny an answer, Ned went as far as to concoct a vague explanation that Jon's mother was some <a href="/wiki/Smallfolk" title="Smallfolk">lowborn</a> woman named "<a href="/wiki/Wylla" title="Wylla">Wylla</a>" that he met during the war.<sup id="cite_ref-E02_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E02-6">[7]</a></sup> Lady Catelyn's eldest son, <a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">Robb</a>, would be acknowledged unquestionably as Eddard's heir, but Jon was otherwise never treated much differently than her younger sons <a href="/wiki/Bran_Stark" title="Bran Stark">Bran</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rickon_Stark" title="Rickon Stark">Rickon</a>.
</p><p>Despite sharing a happy marriage, Jon's presence at Winterfell would serve as a constant source of friction between Eddard and Catelyn. Because Jon was never <a href="/wiki/Legitimization" title="Legitimization">legitimized</a>, Catelyn was never his "stepmother" in any sense of the term or had any obligations to him whatsoever. She never mistreated Jon but she was cold towards him and avoided him whenever possible, viewing him only as a living reminder of the one time that Eddard had dishonored her.<sup id="cite_ref-E01_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E01-7">[8]</a></sup> Catelyn would later confess to her daughter-in-law <a href="/wiki/Talisa_Stark" title="Talisa Stark">Talisa</a> about how Jon caught the pox when he was a child, and she stayed with him through the night and prayed to the gods to let him live out of guilt for previously praying for his death, accepting that the boy was not to blame for her husband's sin, though it was still not enough to make her love Jon, something she would eventually come to regret.<sup id="cite_ref-E22_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E22-8">[9]</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his bastard status, Jon grew up feeling like an outsider at Winterfell. Although Lord Stark would see that he was well-treated, Jon's attendance at Winterfell's more "formal" occasions was restricted and he would even be barred from sitting inside at the Lord's table with his family so as not to offend important guests.<sup id="cite_ref-E01_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E01-7">[8]</a></sup> Otherwise, Jon still lived better than many bastard-born children and was well-raised by Eddard as his own. He was loved by his father and siblings, was never hungry or poor, lived in his father's castle, and had a noble's upbringing. Jon received a highborn education from Maester <a href="/wiki/Luwin" title="Luwin">Luwin</a> and a young lord's martial training from Winterfell's <a href="/wiki/Master-at-Arms" title="Master-at-Arms">Master-at-Arms</a>, Ser <a href="/wiki/Rodrik_Cassel" title="Rodrik Cassel">Rodrik Cassel</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/35/Jon_and_Robb.png/revision/latest?cb=20140306010939" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Robb"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Robb.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Robb.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/35/Jon_and_Robb.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140306010939"  	 width="180"  	 height="136"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/35/Jon_and_Robb.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140306010939" 	 alt="Jon and Robb"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Robb.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Robb.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="136"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Robb.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Robb play with snowballs in their childhood.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Of the Stark children, Jon was very close friends with Robb - given that they were roughly the same age, being regular companions in training and riding. He was also close with both Bran and Rickon, as well as having a friendly rival in Lord Eddard's <a href="/wiki/Ward" title="Ward">ward</a>, <a href="/wiki/Theon_Greyjoy" title="Theon Greyjoy">Theon Greyjoy</a>. However, Jon's closest relationship was with Lord Stark's younger daughter, <a href="/wiki/Arya_Stark" title="Arya Stark">Arya</a>, who, as an adventurous tomboy prone to un-ladylike pursuits, also felt like a social outsider.<sup id="cite_ref-E02_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E02-6">[7]</a></sup> In contrast, Jon's early relationship with Sansa was unpleasant; very much her mother's daughter, she was aloof and cold to him as well.<sup id="cite_ref-E54_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E54-9">[10]</a></sup>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_1"><a href="/wiki/Season_1" title="Season 1">Season 1</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7d/101_WIC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170526151156" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="101 WIC"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="101_WIC.jpg" 	data-image-name="101 WIC.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7d/101_WIC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526151156"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/7d/101_WIC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526151156" 	 alt="101 WIC"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="101_WIC.jpg" 	data-image-name="101 WIC.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:101_WIC.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon instructs Bran under Ned's watchful eye.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon Snow and Robb instruct Bran in archery, when their father Eddard receives word about a captured <a href="/wiki/Desertion" title="Desertion">deserter</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night's Watch">Night's Watch</a>, for which the penalty is death. Jon accompanies his father, Robb, Bran, Theon, Rodrik, and <a href="/wiki/Jory_Cassel" title="Jory Cassel">Jory Cassel</a>, Rodrik's nephew. out to the holdfast where the deserter, <a href="/wiki/Will" title="Will">Will</a>, is being held. It is Bran's first time watching his father carry out an <a href="/wiki/Execution" title="Execution">execution</a>, but as the deserter is brought into position outside, Jon warns Bran not to look away, as their father will know. Jon praises Bran afterwards for keeping his composure. On their way back to Winterfell, they find a dead <a href="/wiki/Direwolves" title="Direwolves">direwolf</a> - a species not seen south of the Wall in centuries - and her newborn pups.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png/revision/latest?cb=20151228061917" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Screen Shot 2013-06-16 at 12.18.27 AM"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png" 	data-image-name="Screen Shot 2013-06-16 at 12.18.27 AM.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151228061917"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151228061917" 	 alt="Screen Shot 2013-06-16 at 12.18.27 AM"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png" 	data-image-name="Screen Shot 2013-06-16 at 12.18.27 AM.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screen_Shot_2013-06-16_at_12.18.27_AM.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon finds Ghost, the runt of a litter of direwolves.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon talks Lord Eddard into allowing the young Starks to adopt them, pointing out that a direwolf is the <a href="/wiki/Heraldry" title="Heraldry">sigil</a> of House Stark: given that there are five direwolves and five trueborn Stark children, it must be a sign that the Stark children are meant to have the pups. In order to make this point, Jon intentionally leaves himself out of the count of Stark children, and when Bran asks about this, Jon responds that he is not a Stark. Just as they are about to leave, however, he finds the runt of the litter, an albino, which crawled away from its mother's corpse. Theon remarks, "The runt of the litter, that one's yours, Snow." Jon takes this direwolf as his own, naming him <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">Ghost</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/Jon%2C_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png/revision/latest?cb=20120517231826" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon, Robb and Theon 1x01"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon%2C_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png" 	data-image-name="Jon, Robb and Theon 1x01.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/Jon%2C_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120517231826"  	 width="180"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3f/Jon%2C_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120517231826" 	 alt="Jon, Robb and Theon 1x01"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon%2C_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png" 	data-image-name="Jon, Robb and Theon 1x01.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="102"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon,_Robb_and_Theon_1x01.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon, Theon and Robb discuss the royal family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Catelyn ensures that Jon, Robb, and Theon are groomed for the arrival of Robert and Queen <a href="/wiki/Cersei_Lannister" title="Cersei Lannister">Cersei Lannister</a>. Jon, in particular, is set against the altering of his appearance, as well as expressing antipathy against the <a href="/wiki/House_Baratheon_of_King%27s_Landing" title="House Baratheon of King's Landing">royal family</a>. When the Baratheon entourage arrives, Jon is present, but is not allowed to attend the subsequent banquet for fear of offending the royal guests (on Catelyn's suggestion). He waits outside in the courtyard venting his frustrations against a practice dummy. When Jon's uncle, <a href="/wiki/Benjen_Stark" title="Benjen Stark">Benjen Stark</a>, arrives, Jon tells him he has been thinking about it, and before his father leaves for the south he wants to join the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night's Watch">Night's Watch</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e6/Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160730021246" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Winter is Coming Tyrion and Jon"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg" 	data-image-name="Winter is Coming Tyrion and Jon.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e6/Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730021246"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e6/Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730021246" 	 alt="Winter is Coming Tyrion and Jon"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg" 	data-image-name="Winter is Coming Tyrion and Jon.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Winter_is_Coming_Tyrion_and_Jon.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon meets Tyrion Lannister.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Since they don't care about recruits' pasts and even a bastard can rise to positions of high honor in it, the Watch provides an easy escape from his life in Winterfell. He later meets <a href="/wiki/Tyrion_Lannister" title="Tyrion Lannister">Tyrion Lannister</a>, Queen Cersei's younger brother. As a <a href="/wiki/Dwarfism" title="Dwarfism">dwarf</a>, Tyrion knows what it is like to be an outcast, so he gives the young man some advice: never try to hide what he is, for the world will not forget. Instead, he should wear the name "bastard" openly, like armor, and then it can never be used to hurt him. When Jon angrily asks Tyrion what he knows about it, Tyrion replies that "all dwarfs are bastards in their father's eyes."<sup id="cite_ref-E01_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E01-7">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170723145139" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jaime Lannister and Jon Snow 1x02"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jaime Lannister and Jon Snow 1x02.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170723145139"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/17/Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170723145139" 	 alt="Jaime Lannister and Jon Snow 1x02"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jaime Lannister and Jon Snow 1x02.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jaime_Lannister_and_Jon_Snow_1x02.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jaime sarcastically thanks Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before departing, Jon has a run-in with <a href="/wiki/Jaime_Lannister" title="Jaime Lannister">Jaime Lannister</a>, who infamously killed his grandfather <a href="/wiki/Aerys_II_Targaryen" title="Aerys II Targaryen">Aerys II</a>, the Mad King. Jaime sarcastically thanks him for protecting all of them from the mythical monsters that allegedly exist <a href="/wiki/Beyond_the_Wall" title="Beyond the Wall">beyond the Wall</a>, in order to taunt him. Before Jon departs for the Wall, he says goodbye to the unconscious Bran, who has been injured in a fall. He gives Arya a sword named <a href="/wiki/Needle" title="Needle">Needle</a> that he had made especially for her, advising her to "stick them with the pointy end." Jon says he will miss her, and they both hug.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/68/Kingsroad3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110425140718" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Kingsroad3"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Kingsroad3.jpg" 	data-image-name="Kingsroad3.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/68/Kingsroad3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110425140718"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/68/Kingsroad3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110425140718" 	 alt="Kingsroad3"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Kingsroad3.jpg" 	data-image-name="Kingsroad3.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kingsroad3.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Robb bids farewell to Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As he prepares his saddle, Robb asks if Jon said goodbye to Bran and is sure Bran will survive. Jon says Starks are hard to kill, and Robb asks about his mother, and Jon assures him she was kind. Robb offers to visit him at the Wall sometime, and they bid farewell with a hug. At their parting on the <a href="/wiki/Kingsroad" title="Kingsroad">Kingsroad</a>, Eddard vows to tell Jon the truth about his mother the next time they meet. Jon is accompanied by his uncle Benjen and Tyrion, who has expressed a desire to see the Wall (and urinate from the top of it) before he dies. Ghost also accompanies Jon to the Wall.<sup id="cite_ref-E02_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E02-6">[7]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8e/103_LS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170526151049" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="103 LS"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="103_LS.jpg" 	data-image-name="103 LS.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8e/103_LS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526151049"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8e/103_LS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526151049" 	 alt="103 LS"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="103_LS.jpg" 	data-image-name="103 LS.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:103_LS.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon trains at Castle Black.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At <a href="/wiki/Castle_Black" title="Castle Black">Castle Black</a>, Jon's expectations of the Night's Watch are soon disappointed. Instead of a brotherhood of noble warriors sworn to defend the realm from <a href="/wiki/Free_Folk" title="Free Folk">wildlings</a> and <a href="/wiki/White_Walkers" title="White Walkers">White Walkers</a>, he realizes the Watch is a dumping ground for criminals and wastrels. He earns the enmity of Ser <a href="/wiki/Alliser_Thorne" title="Alliser Thorne">Alliser Thorne</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Master-at-Arms" title="Master-at-Arms">Master-at-Arms</a> in charge of training new recruits. He humiliates his fellow recruits with his superior fighting skills, learned from Winterfell's Master-at-Arms over the course of many years.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/54/Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png/revision/latest?cb=20110626074809" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Benjen 1x03"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Benjen 1x03.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/54/Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626074809"  	 width="180"  	 height="116"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/54/Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110626074809" 	 alt="Jon and Benjen 1x03"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Benjen 1x03.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="116"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Benjen_1x03.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Benjen bids farewell to Jon atop the Wall.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Benjen stands with Jon on his first watch and tells him that he is going ranging North of the Wall. Jon is keen to accompany him but Benjen insists that he complete his training. Tyrion helps Jon see that he is no better than the recruits but has been afforded more advantages than them due to his highborn upbringing. Jon offers to train some of his new brothers and <a href="/wiki/Pypar" title="Pypar">Pypar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Grenn" title="Grenn">Grenn</a> accept.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[11]</a></sup> He also befriends the fat and bookish coward <a href="/wiki/Samwell_Tarly" title="Samwell Tarly">Samwell Tarly</a> when he arrives at <a href="/wiki/Castle_Black" title="Castle Black">Castle Black</a> and helps to protect him from the cruelty of Thorne. Thorne angrily tells Jon that going easy on Sam won't help him, and will risk getting him killed during the next winter.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[12]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/64/Jon_1x07.png/revision/latest?cb=20110608214929" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon 1x07"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_1x07.png" 	data-image-name="Jon 1x07.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/64/Jon_1x07.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110608214929"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/64/Jon_1x07.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110608214929" 	 alt="Jon 1x07"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_1x07.png" 	data-image-name="Jon 1x07.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_1x07.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon takes his vows before the heart tree beyond the Wall.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After completing his training, Jon is inducted into the Night's Watch and swears his oath before a weirwood <a href="/wiki/Heart_tree" title="Heart tree">heart tree</a> on the north side of the Wall. He is assigned to the stewards rather than the rangers, and at first, thinks it is due to his ongoing feud with Ser Alliser Thorne. However, Sam points out that Lord Commander <a href="/wiki/Jeor_Mormont" title="Jeor Mormont">Jeor Mormont</a> has asked for Jon as his personal steward, and may be grooming him for command. Jon is concerned when his Uncle Benjen's horse returns to the Wall riderless. Later, Ghost finds the corpses of two rangers assigned to Benjen, <a href="/wiki/Othor" title="Othor">Othor</a> and Ser <a href="/wiki/Jafer_Flowers" title="Jafer Flowers">Jafer Flowers</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">[13]</a></sup> Learning of Eddard's imprisonment in King's Landing, Thorne taunts Jon about being a traitor's bastard, causing Jon to draw a knife in anger. He is restricted to quarters.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/df/Jon_and_Jeor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160823014046" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Jeor"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Jeor.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Jeor.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/df/Jon_and_Jeor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160823014046"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/df/Jon_and_Jeor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160823014046" 	 alt="Jon and Jeor"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Jeor.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Jeor.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Jeor.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lord Commander Mormont rewards Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
Later, Othor's corpse becomes a <a href="/wiki/Wights" title="Wights">wight</a> and attacks Lord Commander Mormont. Jon saves Mormont's life by burning the wight, earning a pardon for his earlier misdemeanor.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[14]</a></sup> Mormont also gives Jon his <a href="/wiki/Valyrian_steel" title="Valyrian steel">Valyrian steel</a> sword, <a href="/wiki/Longclaw" title="Longclaw">Longclaw</a> - given that his own son <a href="/wiki/Jorah_Mormont" title="Jorah Mormont">Jorah</a> fled into exile and left it behind. Jon ponders abandoning the Watch to join Robb's army when it marches against the <a href="/wiki/House_Lannister" title="House Lannister">Lannisters</a>, but Maester <a href="/wiki/Aemon" title="Aemon">Aemon</a> tells him that he chose to stay with the Watch when he was similarly tested - as he is secretly a long-forgotten great uncle of the Mad King, and was once known as Aemon <i>Targaryen</i>, but his entire family was killed at the end of Robert's Rebellion.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">[15]</a></sup><figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/83/Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png/revision/latest?cb=20160730030348" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Pypar 1x10"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Pypar 1x10.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/83/Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730030348"  	 width="180"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/83/Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730030348" 	 alt="Jon and Pypar 1x10"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png" 	data-image-name="Jon and Pypar 1x10.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Pypar_1x10.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon is convinced to return to the Night's Watch.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>News of Eddard's execution reaches Castle Black. Jon immediately leaves, meaning to join Robb and seek vengeance for his father's death. Samwell, Pypar, and Grenn intercept him and convince him to stay. Mormont tells Jon their war against the White Walkers is more important than the game of thrones in <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Landing" title="King's Landing">King's Landing</a>. He tells Jon that the Watch is marching beyond the Wall in force, to find Benjen and learn the truth about the threat. Jon swears to him not to attempt to desert again and accompanies the troops as they set out.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_2"><a href="/wiki/Season_2" title="Season 2">Season 2</a></span></h3>
<p>Lord Commander <a href="/wiki/Jeor_Mormont" title="Jeor Mormont">Jeor Mormont</a> prepares Jon for a command role as the <a href="/wiki/Great_Ranging" title="Great Ranging">Great Ranging</a> travels North seeking <a href="/wiki/Benjen_Stark" title="Benjen Stark">Benjen Stark</a> and an explanation for the wight attack. They pass through several abandoned <a href="/wiki/Wildling" title="Wildling" class="mw-redirect">wildling</a> villages before arriving at the home of their unsavory ally <a href="/wiki/Craster" title="Craster">Craster</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Sam%2C_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160813043828" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Sam, Edd and Jon 2x01"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Sam%2C_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg" 	data-image-name="Sam, Edd and Jon 2x01.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Sam%2C_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160813043828"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/61/Sam%2C_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160813043828" 	 alt="Sam, Edd and Jon 2x01"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Sam%2C_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg" 	data-image-name="Sam, Edd and Jon 2x01.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sam,_Edd_and_Jon_2x01.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Edd tells Jon of Craster's sexual inclinations upon their arrival at the Keep.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon is perplexed when he learns that Craster <a href="/wiki/Incest" title="Incest">incestuously</a> marries his own daughters but apparently has no sons. He takes an instant dislike to Craster when they meet with him. The feeling is mutual but Craster does reveal to Jeor that he has not seen Benjen and that the wildlings are gathering with their leader, <a href="/wiki/King-Beyond-the-Wall" title="King-Beyond-the-Wall">King-Beyond-the-Wall</a> <a href="/wiki/Mance_Rayder" title="Mance Rayder">Mance Rayder</a>. Jeor reprimands Jon for failing to follow his lead with Craster - the man disgusts him as well, but unfortunately, he's one of the few wildlings who is willing to give them shelter and supplies which mean the difference between life and death for many black brothers in the wild.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[17]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Samwell_Tarly" title="Samwell Tarly">Samwell Tarly</a> appeals to Jon to aid Craster's pregnant daughter-wife <a href="/wiki/Gilly" title="Gilly">Gilly</a>. She is afraid of having a son but will not say why. Jon is frustrated and refuses to disobey Jeor's order to leave Craster's wives alone. Jon sees Craster carrying a newborn into the woods and follows him. He sees Craster leave the child for a <a href="/wiki/White_Walker_(The_Night_Lands)" title="White Walker (The Night Lands)">White Walker</a> but does not recognize the creature hidden in the shadows. Craster spots him and knocks him out.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[18]</a></sup> Craster disarms Jon and drags him back to his keep. He expels the rangers from his home. Jeor reveals that he knew that Craster was sacrificing his sons but chose to ignore it because of his usefulness as an ally of the Night's Watch.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[19]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/39/Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120529144736" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Arriving at the fist of the first men"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg" 	data-image-name="Arriving at the fist of the first men.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/39/Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120529144736"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/39/Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120529144736" 	 alt="Arriving at the fist of the first men"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg" 	data-image-name="Arriving at the fist of the first men.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Arriving_at_the_fist_of_the_first_men.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon arrives at the Fist of the First Men.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>The rangers reach the ancient fortified peak known as the <a href="/wiki/Fist_of_the_First_Men" title="Fist of the First Men">Fist of the First Men</a> and await <a href="/wiki/Qhorin_Halfhand" title="Qhorin Halfhand" class="mw-redirect">Qhorin Halfhand</a> and his party from the <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Tower" title="Shadow Tower" class="mw-redirect">Shadow Tower</a>. When Qhorin arrives he suggests altering their tactics and using small groups to overcome Mance's lookouts in the <a href="/wiki/Skirling_Pass" title="Skirling Pass">Skirling Pass</a>. Jon asks to join Qhorin's raiders and Jeor lets him go.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">[20]</a></sup>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1d/Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png/revision/latest?cb=20160719041839" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon lies with Ygritte 2x6"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png" 	data-image-name="Jon lies with Ygritte 2x6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1d/Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719041839"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1d/Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719041839" 	 alt="Jon lies with Ygritte 2x6"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png" 	data-image-name="Jon lies with Ygritte 2x6.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_lies_with_Ygritte_2x6.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Ygritte share body heat.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Qhorin leads his men into the pass and they locate and ambush the wildling watchers. Jon realizes his opponent is a young woman and hesitates to kill her. She introduces herself as <a href="/wiki/Ygritte" title="Ygritte">Ygritte</a> but does not give away details of Mance's plans. Qhorin leaves Jon alone to execute Ygritte. Jon is unable to do it and she escapes. He pursues and recaptures her but they become separated from Qhorin's group. Jon decides they cannot regroup with Qhorin due to the approaching night. Ygritte convinces Jon to sleep next to her to share body heat and keep warm, and then makes sexual advances towards him. Jon rejects the temptation to break his oath.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[21]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e4/Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160719232821" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Ygritte"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Ygritte.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e4/Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719232821"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e4/Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719232821" 	 alt="Jon and Ygritte"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Ygritte.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Ygritte.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Ygritte discuss the restrictions of the Night's Watch vows, including his virginity.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As he unties Ygrittes legs to continue his search for the rest of the raiders, she tells him that she knows that he is a virgin. He uses some the rope thats binding her as a leash. As they walk, Ygritte questions Jon as to why the men of the Night's Watch hate the wildlings. She explains that both the <a href="/wiki/Free_Folk" title="Free Folk">wildlings</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Northmen" title="Northmen">Northmen</a> like the Starks are descendants of the <a href="/wiki/First_Men" title="First Men">First Men</a>, and the wildlings just happened to be on the wrong side of the Wall when it was built. She urges him to forget about his oath and live free. Another sexual advance from Ygritte prompts him to reach for his sword. She backs away and trips him with the rope when he is caught off guard.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9d/Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160720012454" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Halfhand and Jon Snow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Halfhand and Jon Snow.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9d/Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160720012454"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9d/Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160720012454" 	 alt="Halfhand and Jon Snow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Halfhand and Jon Snow.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Halfhand_and_Jon_Snow.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Qhorin and Jon are held captive by the wildlings.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He pursues her but is ambushed and taken captive. Ygritte tells him that he should have taken her when he had the chance.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[22]</a></sup> Ygritte brings Jon to the <a href="/wiki/Lord_of_Bones" title="Lord of Bones">Lord of Bones</a> and convinces him that Mance will want to question Jon. The Lord of Bones has a prisoner of his own; Qhorin. The Halfhand tells Jon that the rest of the men were killed while they searched for him. He urges Jon to make their deaths meaningful and become a spy within the wildling ranks. He then feigns anger with Jon until he is restrained after managing to knock Jon over.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">[23]</a></sup>
</p><p>In Winterfell, after Theon Greyjoy betrays House Stark and takes the castle, he refuses to flee and join the Night's Watch when he is surrounded by <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_Snow" title="Ramsay Snow" class="mw-redirect">Ramsay Snow</a>'s men on the basis that Jon will likely kill him for betraying the Starks and apparently burning Bran and Rickon alive (in actuality, Theon faked their deaths following their escape, in order to intimidate his northern subjects).<sup id="cite_ref-E20_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E20-23">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cc/Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160720032340" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon kills Qhorin"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon kills Qhorin.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cc/Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160720032340"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cc/Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160720032340" 	 alt="Jon kills Qhorin"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon kills Qhorin.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_kills_Qhorin.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon slays Qhorin.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>As they make their way to Mance, Ygritte continues to playfully mock Jon by tapping him on the head with the flat of Longclaw. Qhorin uses the distraction to advance his plan to portray Jon as a traitor to the Night's Watch. He attacks Jon, and the Lord of Bones allows them to fight. Jon is initially reluctant until Qhorin calls <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">his "father"</a> a traitor and his mother a whore. Jon slays Qhorin, who whispers a line from the Night's Watch oath to Jon with his dying breath, stunning Ygritte and the rest of the band. Jon's hands are freed, and Ygritte leads him to the crest of the mountain to look over the massive wildling encampment.<sup id="cite_ref-E20_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E20-23">[24]</a></sup>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_3"><a href="/wiki/Season_3" title="Season 3">Season 3</a></span></h3>
<p>As Jon is led by Ygritte and the Lord of Bones into the main wildling camp in the <a href="/wiki/Frostfangs" title="Frostfangs">Frostfang mountains</a>, he discovers that almost all of wildling society is on the move to escape the White Walkers, including the women and children. As they enter the camp, Jon is shocked to see a real-life <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giant</a> walk past. Many of the wildlings are surprised to see Jon in his all-black Night's Watch clothing and shout "crow!" at his approach. Several young boys pelt Jon with ice and small stones but Ygritte shoos them away.<sup id="cite_ref-E21_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E21-24">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon is led into the tent of the King-Beyond-the-Wall, <a href="/wiki/Mance_Rayder" title="Mance Rayder">Mance Rayder</a>, where the Lord of Bones explains that he is Ned Stark's bastard son to a large man with a heavy beard who is eating chicken by the fire. He says he doesn't care, but his interest is piqued on hearing that Jon killed Qhorin Halfhand. As they talk Jon kneels before the man, whom he assumes to be Mance Rayder, and calls him "your Grace". This causes all of the wildlings to burst out laughing. As it turns out this isn't Mance, but his lieutenant <a href="/wiki/Tormund" title="Tormund">Tormund Giantsbane</a>. The real Mance is an unassuming man sitting in a corner, who then introduces himself and tells Jon to stand, as no man kneels before another among the <a href="/wiki/Free_Folk" title="Free Folk">Free Folk</a>, since they do not recognize a class of nobility in their culture.<sup id="cite_ref-E21_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E21-24">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>Mance says he is glad that Jon killed Qhorin, as he had killed many of Mance's wildlings. Mance asks Jon why he wants to join them and he replies he wants to be free, but Mance doesn't believe this. Jon then explains that when the Night's Watch camped at <a href="/wiki/Craster%27s_Keep" title="Craster's Keep">Craster's Keep</a>, he saw Craster leave his newborn son in the woods as an offering, and the inhuman creature that took it. Jon says that he wants to leave the Night's Watch because he is disgusted that Mormont already knew what Craster was doing but did nothing to stop it. Jon states that the <a href="/wiki/First_Men" title="First Men">First Men</a> he is descended from defeated the White Walkers once during the <a href="/wiki/Long_Night" title="Long Night">Long Night</a>, and that now he wants "to fight for the side who fights for the living". Mance is satisfied and advises Jon to get a new cloak, his black one clearly attracting malignity.<sup id="cite_ref-E21_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E21-24">[25]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130609163935" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg" 	data-image-name="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130609163935"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130609163935" 	 alt="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg" 	data-image-name="Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Got-game-of-thrones-34037192-953-536.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Mance explains his unification process to Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon Snow then marches south with the Free Folk army and Mance Rayder. Mance explains that his army is a diverse force, formed of about ninety different groups or clans of wildlings, who speak seven different languages, and have numerous internal rivalries. However, he managed to unite them all by telling them the truth: that they will all die if they remain north of the Wall. Mance brings Jon to one of his scouts, <a href="/wiki/Orell" title="Orell">Orell</a>. He is sitting silently with his eyes rolled back as an eagle circles above him. Mance says that he is a "<a href="/wiki/Warg" title="Warg">warg</a>".
</p><p>Jon, ignorant to what a warg is, explained to that a warg is a person who is capable of entering the mind of an animal, seeing what it sees and even controlling its actions. Orell controls his eagle to scout miles ahead. Mance asks him what he has seen, and Orell says he saw the Fist of the First Men - and many dead "crows".<sup id="cite_ref-E22_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E22-8">[9]</a></sup>
</p><p>As Jon Snow and the Free Folk arrive at the Fist of the First Men, they survey the bloody aftermath of the assault on the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night's Watch">Night's Watch</a> by the White Walkers and their army of undead <a href="/wiki/Wights" title="Wights">wights</a>. However, they only find corpses of <a href="/wiki/Horses" title="Horses">horses</a> and no human remains. Jon says that there were three hundred men of the Night's Watch at the Fist, and asks Mance if Mormont could still be alive. Mance says that with Mormont, it's possible he was able to escape, but that even if he did he and his men took quite a beating and are trapped miles away from the Wall with the White Walkers in close pursuit. Mance warns Jon that all of the missing corpses from the Fist are no longer his friends and brothers from the Night's Watch, but have been resurrected as undead monsters who serve the White Walkers. Jon reluctantly agrees.<sup id="cite_ref-E23_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E23-25">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Mance orders Tormund to take a force of twenty men to scale the Wall to attack Castle Black from its exposed rear. Mance's plan is for Tormund's small band to distract Castle Black by attacking their exposed southern side, at which point Mance's main army will assault it from the north. Tormund will know that Mance is in position when his army makes a massive signal fire. Mance orders Tormund to take Jon with him, as Jon knows the layout of Castle Black, and it will prove a key test of his loyalty: if it turns out that he won't really betray the Night's Watch, Tormund can easily throw him off the Wall to his death.<sup id="cite_ref-E23_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E23-25">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>On their way to the Wall and Castle Black, Jon and Ygritte are gathering firewood, when the warg Orell asks him about the defenses of the Night's Watch. Orell has seen through the eyes of his eagle that there are patrols on top of the Wall and he wants to know how frequent they are. Jon says they usually sent out patrols in teams of four, two builders to inspect for structural damage and two rangers to protect them, but that the frequency of their patrols often changes. Orell says the wildlings know there are nineteen castles along the south side of the Wall, but he wants to know how many are currently manned.
</p><p>Jon finds this very unpleasant, but reluctantly says that only three are currently manned. Apart from Castle Black, there is also <a href="/wiki/Eastwatch-by-the-Sea" title="Eastwatch-by-the-Sea">Eastwatch-by-the-Sea</a> at the extreme eastern end, and the <a href="/wiki/Shadow_Tower" title="Shadow Tower" class="mw-redirect">Shadow Tower</a> at the western end. Jon is then asked how many men currently garrison Castle Black. Jon is very reluctant to answer, but after being threatened by Orell, he gives an exaggerated number, saying there are one thousand men (this is a lie, as Castle Black only had six hundred men before the Great Ranging, and the garrison now is closer to three hundred). Tormund tells Jon that he likes him, but if he is lying to them, he will rip his guts out through his throat. Despite this, Jon remains steadfast to the lie.<sup id="cite_ref-E25_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E25-26">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/43/Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png/revision/latest?cb=20160809141722" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png" 	data-image-name="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/43/Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809141722"  	 width="180"  	 height="99"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/43/Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809141722" 	 alt="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png" 	data-image-name="Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="99"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kissed-by-fire-jon-and-ygritte.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon looses his virginity to Ygritte.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and Ygritte then walk away, but she steals his sword Longclaw, making him chase her to get it back. She leads him into a nearby cave. Ygritte starts disrobing, and says that she wants to make sure Jon Snow has truly come over to the wildlings' side and broken his Night's Watch vows - by making him break his oath of celibacy with her. She quickly shucks off all of her clothes and walks up to him naked. Jon is very hesitant at first, but they soon end up having sex in the cave.<sup id="cite_ref-E25_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E25-26">[27]</a></sup> Afterwards Jon and Ygritte lay together in a naked embrace and Ygritte tells Jon she wishes they could stay in this cave forever.<sup id="cite_ref-E25_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E25-26">[27]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130506182652" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Ygritte kissing"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Ygritte kissing.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130506182652"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130506182652" 	 alt="Jon and Ygritte kissing"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Ygritte kissing.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Ygritte_kissing.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Ygritte kiss atop the Wall.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He joins a wildling party led by Tormund Giantsbane to climb the Wall. Beforehand, he is questioned by Ygritte about their relationship and his allegiance to the Night's Watch, saying that he must be loyal to her instead. During the climb, Ygritte causes part of the ice to break, leaving them hanging in the air by the rope. Orell, believing them to be lost, cuts it. Jon manages to save himself and Ygritte by climbing back to the ice. The two return to the climb and reach the top, where Ygritte gazes at the north side and the south side, before they kiss.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[28]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d1/Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130513044455" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Ygritte and Jon Bear and Maiden Fair"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg" 	data-image-name="Ygritte and Jon Bear and Maiden Fair.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d1/Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130513044455"  	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d1/Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130513044455" 	 alt="Ygritte and Jon Bear and Maiden Fair"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg" 	data-image-name="Ygritte and Jon Bear and Maiden Fair.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ygritte_and_Jon_Bear_and_Maiden_Fair.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Ygritte journey south of the Wall.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After surviving the perilous climb of the Wall, Jon Snow, Ygritte and the wildlings led by Tormund Giantsbane advance through <a href="/wiki/The_Gift" title="The Gift">the Gift</a> - the strip of land immediately south of the Wall which the Watch draws supplies from - and continue on towards Castle Black, to await Mance Rayder's signal to begin the attack. Afterwards, Jon confronts Orell about cutting his and Ygritte's rope loose on the Wall, nearly killing both of them in the process. Orell tells Jon that he doesn't see Ygritte complaining about what happened because she is a wildling and understood what needed to be done in a pressure situation, also telling Jon that this is the reason he will never be able to keep her.
</p><p>During the journey through the woods, a clearly jealous Orell confronts Ygritte and says that he would be a better man for her than Jon Snow, while continuing to express his distrust in him. Jon also tries to persuade Ygritte that the wildlings' cause is doomed to failure, but she refuses to listen and points out that Jon is technically one of them; if it fails, so does he. She restates her passion for him and tells him bluntly that if they die, they die, but before they die they will live.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">[29]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/bb/Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png/revision/latest?cb=20140602175855" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Ygritte and Jon - The Rains of Castamere"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png" 	data-image-name="Ygritte and Jon - The Rains of Castamere.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/bb/Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602175855"  	 width="180"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/bb/Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602175855" 	 alt="Ygritte and Jon - The Rains of Castamere"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png" 	data-image-name="Ygritte and Jon - The Rains of Castamere.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ygritte_and_Jon_-_The_Rains_of_Castamere.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Ygritte argue over the killing of innocents.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and the wildling party prepare to raid an elderly horse breeder's home for his horses and gold; Jon insists that the old man is no threat to them, but Orell and Tormund Giantsbane intend to kill the man so as to stop him from alerting the Night's Watch to their presence. However, when the party attacks the farmstead, Jon surreptitiously hits a rock with his sword, alerting the old man who flees; Jon also distracts Ygritte when she tries to shoot the fleeing man with an arrow. Outside, Tormund moves to kill the old man, but Orell tells him to have Jon do it instead to prove his loyalty. Jon is ultimately unable to kill the innocent man, and instead, Ygritte kills the man with an arrow.
</p>
