<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png/revision/latest?cb=20130603044951" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Rain of castamere jon snow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png" 	data-image-name="Rain of castamere jon snow.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130603044951"  	 width="180"  	 height="110"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130603044951" 	 alt="Rain of castamere jon snow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png" 	data-image-name="Rain of castamere jon snow.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="110"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rain_of_castamere_jon_snow.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon battles Orell.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Realizing that Jon is still loyal to the Night's Watch, Tormund orders his men to kill Jon; Tormund restrains Ygritte to stop her trying to help Jon, and soon after Jon battles with Orell. In the nearby <a href="/wiki/Queenscrown" title="Queenscrown">Queenscrown</a>, a hidden Bran enters the mind of <a href="/wiki/Summer" title="Summer">Summer</a> to aid Jon. as he battles to the death with Orell and finally kills him. With the last of his strength Orell wargs into the mind of his pet eagle, which swoops down and attacks Jon, clawing him badly about the face before he fights the bird off. Jon then steals a horse and escapes, leaving a heartbroken Ygritte and heading back to the Wall.<sup id="cite_ref-E29_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E29-29">[30]</a></sup>
</p><p>Stopping to rest and tend to his injury, Jon is confronted by a furious Ygritte, who has an arrow ready to shoot him. Jon tries to talk Ygritte out of shooting him, insisting that he still loves her. Though his feelings are clearly reciprocated Ygritte is still angered by his betrayal and shoots Jon three times with her bow as he flees from her. Jon is badly injured, but his horse manages to carry him the rest of the way to Castle Black, as he hovers in and out of consciousness. Having reached safety, Jon is brought inside the castle by the guards, where he encounters Sam and Pypar, who are overjoyed to see him and insist that his injuries be taken care of.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">[31]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_4"><a href="/wiki/Season_4" title="Season 4">Season 4</a></span></h3>
<p>Jon survives the injuries inflicted by Ygritte and has largely recovered, though he still grimaces while getting dressed. At some point, Jon has been told about his half-brother Robb's death at the <a href="/wiki/Red_Wedding" title="Red Wedding">Red Wedding</a> and wanting vengeance for his family, but decides to stay at the wall. He shares with Sam that he had always been jealous of Robb for having more of their father's affection and for being better than him at riding, fighting, and winning the affection of other girls. Still, he says he could never bring himself to hate Robb, as he was also always a good friend and honorable person. Sam responds by saying he has felt the same way about Jon, that Jon is better than him at everything (except reading).
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/14/S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png/revision/latest?cb=20140607081242" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E1 - Jon Snow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png" 	data-image-name="S04E1 - Jon Snow.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/14/S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140607081242"  	 width="180"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/14/S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140607081242" 	 alt="S04E1 - Jon Snow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png" 	data-image-name="S04E1 - Jon Snow.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="106"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E1_-_Jon_Snow.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon testifies before a panel of sworn brothers.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>It turns out that Sam had been sent to retrieve Jon, who has been summoned to testify before a panel of five sworn brothers, including Maester <a href="/wiki/Aemon" title="Aemon">Aemon</a>, acting Lord Commander Alliser Thorne, and <a href="/wiki/Janos_Slynt" title="Janos Slynt">Janos Slynt</a> (who was exiled to the Wall by Tyrion). At the hearing Jon admits to killing Qhorin Halfhand, to living amongst the wildlings, and even to having bedded one. He also states that Mance intends to attack and gives intel on his plans and strength. Both Slynt and Thorne are openly hostile to Jon, disbelieving much of what he says and call for his execution. Aemon, however, realizes that Jon is speaking the truth, and the hearing ends with Jon being allowed to keep his head.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[32]</a></sup>
</p><p>Meanwhile, at the <a href="/wiki/Dreadfort" title="Dreadfort" class="mw-redirect">Dreadfort</a>, when Theon Greyjoy is pressed by <a href="/wiki/Roose_Bolton" title="Roose Bolton">Roose Bolton</a> for information on the whereabouts of Bran and Rickon Stark, he reluctantly guesses that they may try to head to Jon at Castle Black. On <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_Snow" title="Ramsay Snow" class="mw-redirect">Ramsay Snow</a>'s suggestion, Jon becomes a target of the Boltons, since Ramsay reasons that even though Jon may be a bastard, he is still a son of Ned Stark, and may pose a threat to the Boltons' future hold on the North, either because the Northerners who are still furious at the Boltons for betraying the Starks may rally behind him even though he is a bastard in the Night's Watch, or because Jon may simply seek revenge on both Roose and Ramsay for their role in the Starks' downfall at Red Wedding. Roose subsequently sends his hunter, <a href="/wiki/Locke" title="Locke">Locke</a>, to the Wall in order to infiltrate the Watch, use Jon to find Bran and Rickon and then kill them all, promising a lordship as a reward.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[33]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c2/Jon_speaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20160730033009" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon speaks"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_speaks.png" 	data-image-name="Jon speaks.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c2/Jon_speaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730033009"  	 width="180"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c2/Jon_speaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730033009" 	 alt="Jon speaks"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_speaks.png" 	data-image-name="Jon speaks.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_speaks.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon speaks to the Night's Watch about the wildling threat following the raids in the Gift.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The orphan <a href="/wiki/Olly" title="Olly">Olly</a> then arrives at Castle black, telling them how the wildling raiding parties south of the Wall killed his entire village. Thorne asks for Jon's opinion on protecting the <a href="/wiki/Smallfolk" title="Smallfolk">smallfolk</a> living in <a href="/wiki/The_Gift" title="The Gift">the Gift</a>, thinking Jon will disagree with his decision not to send help. Instead, Jon regretfully says that he knows from his time with the wildlings that this exactly what they want - to lure as many of them out of Castle Black as possible to weaken its defenses for the massive attack about to come from the north side of the Wall, which would allow them to move over a thousand miles southward before they reached an army that could stop them.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/59/403_BOC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170526145121" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="403 BOC"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="403_BOC.jpg" 	data-image-name="403 BOC.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/59/403_BOC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526145121"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/59/403_BOC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170526145121" 	 alt="403 BOC"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="403_BOC.jpg" 	data-image-name="403 BOC.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:403_BOC.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon is informed as the situation at Craster's Keep, potentially giving the wildlings an advantage.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Therefore, Jon agrees with Thorne that they should do nothing, and concentrate every available man in Castle Black itself to brace for the assault. They are interrupted by a single horn blast, revealed to be Grenn and Edd, who have escaped the <a href="/wiki/Betrayers" title="Betrayers" class="mw-redirect">mutineers</a> at Craster's Keep. Jon is relieved to see them alive, but his relief turns to concern when they reveal that the mutineers remain entrenched at the keep. Jon understands that if the mutineers are captured by Mance Rayder, then the wildlings will know how vulnerable Castle Black really is. Jon tries to convince Alliser Thorne that eliminating the mutineers should be their top priority.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[34]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png/revision/latest?cb=20160719015349" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Grenn and Jon - Oathkeeper"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png" 	data-image-name="Grenn and Jon - Oathkeeper.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719015349"  	 width="180"  	 height="126"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719015349" 	 alt="Grenn and Jon - Oathkeeper"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png" 	data-image-name="Grenn and Jon - Oathkeeper.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="126"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Grenn_and_Jon_-_Oathkeeper.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Grenn train the new recruits in preparation for the impending battle against the wildlings.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and Grenn are training the new recruits, one of which is Locke, to fight wildlings. The training session is interrupted by Thorne who continues to talk down to Jon and reminds him that he is a steward. Locke approaches Jon and they get acquainted, with Jon unaware of Locke's true purpose. Jon and Sam are talking about Bran going beyond the Wall. Jon is worried for Bran and once he realizes that he could be at Craster's Keep, Locke comes in to tell him that Thorne has summoned him. Thorne gives him permission to attack Craster's Keep, but only with volunteers (Slynt convinced Thorne that Jon questioning his decisions is a problem, and if Jon gets himself killed on a dangerous mission he <i>volunteered</i> for (knowing the risks), it will both remove him and be his own fault; alternatively, if he succeeds and returns alive, so much the better).
</p><p>Jon gives a speech about avenging Mormont's death at the hands of the mutineers and this convinces a number of his brothers to join him in his attack, including Grenn, Edd, and Locke (who secretly intends to kill Jon during the mission and blame it on the mutineers).<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">[35]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6b/Karl%27s_death.png/revision/latest?cb=20160809201532" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Karl&amp;#039;s death"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Karl%27s_death.png" 	data-image-name="Karl&#39;s death.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6b/Karl%27s_death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809201532"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6b/Karl%27s_death.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809201532" 	 alt="Karl&amp;#039;s death"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Karl%27s_death.png" 	data-image-name="Karl&#39;s death.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Karl%27s_death.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon kills Karl with Longclaw.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The group <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Craster%27s_Keep" title="Raid on Craster's Keep">attacks</a> at night, taking the mutineers by surprise. Jon personally enters the main building to deal with <a href="/wiki/Karl_Tanner" title="Karl Tanner">Karl Tanner</a>. The two of them are evenly matched, though Karl manages to get the upper hand by spitting in Jon's face and then kicking him to the floor. Before he can land the finishing blow, Karl is stabbed in the back by <a href="/wiki/Sissy" title="Sissy">Sissy</a>. Karl attempts to kill her, though it's a fatal mistake as Jon doesn't miss the opportunity to thrust Longclaw through the back of Karl's head and out of his mouth.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png/revision/latest?cb=20160723031647" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E5 - Jon Snow &amp;amp; Ghost"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png" 	data-image-name="S04E5 - Jon Snow &amp;amp; Ghost.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031647"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031647" 	 alt="S04E5 - Jon Snow &amp;amp; Ghost"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png" 	data-image-name="S04E5 - Jon Snow &amp;amp; Ghost.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E5_-_Jon_Snow_%26_Ghost.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon reunites with Ghost.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the fight, Jon and the others count five dead amongst the Watch, including Locke, whose neck was snapped in a way that terrifies Jon (Jon being completely unaware that Locke had been killed by a Bran-possessed <a href="/wiki/Hodor" title="Hodor">Hodor</a>). He then reunites with Ghost before turning to Craster's wives and offering them refuge at Castle Black. They decline, saying that after the abuse they took at other members of the Night's Watch they can't trust them and will go their own way. Before leaving, they set a torch to Craster's Keep, burning it to the ground.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">[36]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/47/S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png/revision/latest?cb=20160811100747" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E7 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png" 	data-image-name="S04E7 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/47/S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160811100747"  	 width="180"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/47/S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160811100747" 	 alt="S04E7 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png" 	data-image-name="S04E7 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="114"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E7_-_Jon_%26_Grenn.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon returns to Castle Black.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and his fellow black brothers return to Castle Black, much to the annoyance of Ser Alliser Thorne and Janos Slynt. Once Alliser spots Ghost, he orders Jon to lock up Ghost or his direwolf will become food for the Night's Watch. Later, Jon reports that Mance Rayder's army was closing in on Craster's Keep and will reach the Wall before the next full moon. Jon states that defending the tunnel is hopeless since the gates will not stop the giants in Mance Rayder's army. He proposes they seal the tunnel, but Alliser Thorne refuses to listen. Alliser then assigns Jon and Samwell Tarly to night duties atop the Wall until the next new moon.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[37]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png/revision/latest?cb=20160723031706" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E8 - Jon &amp;amp; Sam"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png" 	data-image-name="S04E8 - Jon &amp;amp; Sam.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031706"  	 width="180"  	 height="107"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031706" 	 alt="S04E8 - Jon &amp;amp; Sam"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png" 	data-image-name="S04E8 - Jon &amp;amp; Sam.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="107"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E8_-_Jon_%26_Sam.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Sam receive the recent news regarding Mole's Town.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>News of the wildling <a href="/wiki/Sack_of_Mole%27s_Town" title="Sack of Mole's Town">attack on Mole's Town</a>, the largest village in the Gift, reaches Castle Black. Jon, Pypar, and Eddison Tollett try to comfort a distraught Sam, who believes that <a href="/wiki/Gilly" title="Gilly">Gilly</a> and her baby are dead. Grenn is furious that the wildlings slaughtered the inhabitants of <a href="/wiki/Mole%27s_Town" title="Mole's Town">Mole's Town</a>, which included brothers of the Night's Watch. Jon concludes that if Mole's Town has been attacked, then Mance Rayder's assault on Castle Black is imminent.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[38]</a></sup>
</p><p>Atop the Wall, Jon and Sam are staring out into the darkness of the north and awaiting the imminent wildling invasion. Sam attempts to interrogate Jon about what it was like to be with a woman, stating that as their deaths are likely imminent, it may be his last chance to find out. Sam brings up that the vows of the Night's Watch only explicitly forbid members from taking wives or producing children, and that other "activities" are open to interpretation. Jon replies glumly that Ser Alliser most likely does not care about their interpretations. When further pressed by Sam to describe lying down with Ygritte, Jon attempts to explain but is unable to properly express it, proclaiming exasperatedly that he is "not a bleeding poet." Jon offers to take the watch up alone so Sam can go below.<sup id="cite_ref-E39_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E39-38">[39]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/da/S04E09_-_Jon_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20160723031842" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E09 - Jon (On the Wall)"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E09_-_Jon_%28On_the_Wall%29.png" 	data-image-name="S04E09 - Jon (On the Wall).png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/da/S04E09_-_Jon_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031842"  	 width="180"  	 height="113"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/da/S04E09_-_Jon_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160723031842" 	 alt="S04E09 - Jon (On the Wall)"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E09_-_Jon_%28On_the_Wall%29.png" 	data-image-name="S04E09 - Jon (On the Wall).png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="113"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E09_-_Jon_(On_the_Wall).png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon spots Mance's promised signal.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later that night, Jon hears the horn blowing and looks north, witnessing a tremendous conflagration north of the Wall, just as Mance had promised him. Jon approaches Thorne, who finally relents and admits that they should have heeded his advice and sealed the tunnel, but grimly muses that leadership means not second-guessing oneself because of "clever little twats" like him. While they start to prepare for the massive wildling army that is emerging from the woods, another horn blows from down below at Castle Black, signaling the unanticipated appearance of Tormund's band of wildlings at Castle Black.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d4/S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20160730064937" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E09 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn (On the Wall)"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_%28On_the_Wall%29.png" 	data-image-name="S04E09 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn (On the Wall).png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d4/S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730064937"  	 width="180"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d4/S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_%28On_the_Wall%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730064937" 	 alt="S04E09 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn (On the Wall)"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_%28On_the_Wall%29.png" 	data-image-name="S04E09 - Jon &amp;amp; Grenn (On the Wall).png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E09_-_Jon_%26_Grenn_(On_the_Wall).png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon silently thanks Grenn.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Alliser decides to go down and defend the keep, leaving Janos Slynt in charge of the Wall's defenses. Even though a wildling strike force led by two giants, <a href="/wiki/Mag_Mar_Tun_Doh_Weg" title="Mag Mar Tun Doh Weg">one of which</a> is riding a <a href="/wiki/Mammoths" title="Mammoths">mammoth</a>, charge towards Castle Black's outer gate, Janos Slynt does nothing and breaks down, demoralizing the troops. Grenn steps in by falsely claiming that Alliser needs Janos back down in Castle Black, allowing Jon to take command of the Wall's defenses, silently thanking Grenn.<sup id="cite_ref-E39_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E39-38">[39]</a></sup> The black brothers continue to rain down arrows on the advancing wildlings, even killing ones that are attempting to scale the Wall.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140609125040" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg" 	data-image-name="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140609125040"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/05/Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140609125040" 	 alt="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg" 	data-image-name="Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Season-4-Episode-9-The-Watchers-on-the-Wall-game-of-thrones-37169832-2100-1397.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon takes command on the northern defense.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Giant_(The_Watchers_on_the_Wall)" title="Giant (The Watchers on the Wall)" class="mw-redirect">One giant</a>, armed with a massive bow, manages to fire a huge arrow at one of the bunkers atop the Wall, and Jon is unable to warn his brothers fast enough before the giant fires again, violently killing one of his black brothers. Although Jon manages to repel most of the wildlings attacking the outer gate, including the mammoth, one giant manages to single-handedly lift the gate. Jon, knowing the inner gate won't hold against him, sends a group of black brothers led by Grenn to hold it at any cost. Jon decides to give Edd control of the top of the Wall, and tasks Sam with releasing <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">Ghost</a> from his pen to assist in the fighting, then orders half a dozen other men to descend with him and finally enter the fray.<sup id="cite_ref-E39_38-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E39-38">[39]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6f/Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140611211338" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of Castle Black"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of Castle Black.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6f/Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140611211338"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6f/Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140611211338" 	 alt="Battle of Castle Black"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of Castle Black.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_Castle_Black.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon fights Styr during the Battle of Castle Black.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon quickly dispatches many wildlings with Longclaw, catching the attention of <a href="/wiki/Styr" title="Styr">Styr</a>, Magnar of the <a href="/wiki/Thenns" title="Thenns">Thenns</a>, and so the two meet in single combat. Styr eventually gets the upper hand by knocking Longclaw away, then Jon disarms Styr of his axe using some chains, and the fighting goes hand to hand. Styr brutally smashes his face into an anvil and tosses him into the blacksmith's forge. However, when Styr picks Jon up and begins to strangle him, Jon spits blood in Styr's face, distracting him long enough for him to grab the blacksmith's hammer lying next to him and bury it into Styr's skull.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/40/Ygritte_dies.png/revision/latest?cb=20160719042121" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Ygritte dies"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_dies.png" 	data-image-name="Ygritte dies.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/40/Ygritte_dies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719042121"  	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/40/Ygritte_dies.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160719042121" 	 alt="Ygritte dies"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Ygritte_dies.png" 	data-image-name="Ygritte dies.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ygritte_dies.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ygritte dies in Jon's arms.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon killing him, Jon turns around to find <a href="/wiki/Ygritte" title="Ygritte">Ygritte</a> pointing her bow at him with an arrow drawn. He smiles at her, causing her to hesitate. Before either can say anything, Ygritte is shot through the heart by Olly. Jon holds her in his arms as she tells him that they should have never left the cave, and they lament circumstances that prevented them from being together as she succumbs to her wound.<sup id="cite_ref-E39_38-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E39-38">[39]</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, while Edd forces the wildling army to retreat for the night, down below Jon deals with a heavily wounded Tormund, who continues to fight despite being the only wildling left alive in the castle. Jon subdues him with a crossbow and orders his brothers to take him prisoner and interrogate him. The following morning, Jon discusses with Sam his suicidal solution to end the wildling threat: he plans to assassinate Mance Rayder, noting that he is the only thing binding the disparate wildling clans that make up the army, and his death will rob them of that purpose and leadership.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/50/Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png/revision/latest?cb=20140615185247" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon goes beyond the Wall"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png" 	data-image-name="Jon goes beyond the Wall.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/50/Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140615185247"  	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/50/Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140615185247" 	 alt="Jon goes beyond the Wall"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png" 	data-image-name="Jon goes beyond the Wall.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_goes_beyond_the_Wall.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon ventures beyond the Wall to confront Mance.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sam tries to stop him, but to no avail. As Jon prepares to leave via Castle Black's tunnel, they discover the bodies of the black brothers who held the inner gate against the giant. Grenn is amongst the casualties and Jon tells Sam that all bodies must be burned. Before Jon leaves, he remembers the promise he made to Jeor Mormont and decides to leave Longclaw with Sam. Sam tells Jon to come back, and Jon looks and Sam and gives him an unsure smile before stepping out into the wilderness on the other side of the gate.<sup id="cite_ref-E39_38-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E39-38">[39]</a></sup> Jon finds Mance in a wildling camp north of the Wall and claims he wants to negotiate with him.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160809105506" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E10 - Jon &amp;amp; Stannis"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg" 	data-image-name="S04E10 - Jon &amp;amp; Stannis.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809105506"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0a/S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809105506" 	 alt="S04E10 - Jon &amp;amp; Stannis"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg" 	data-image-name="S04E10 - Jon &amp;amp; Stannis.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E10_-_Jon_%26_Stannis.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon meets Stannis Baratheon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite Mance expressing disappointment at Jon's betrayal, they drink a toast to some of their fallen friends, such as Grenn, Ygritte, and Mag the giant. Mance then notices that Jon is eyeing a cooking knife, and quickly deduces that Jon came to <a href="/wiki/Parley" title="Parley">parley</a> with Mance simply so he could assassinate him. Before anyone can make a move, they are interrupted by the sound of war horns. Outside, hundreds of mounted knights led by <a href="/wiki/Stannis_Baratheon" title="Stannis Baratheon">Stannis Baratheon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Davos_Seaworth" title="Davos Seaworth">Davos Seaworth</a> arrives and slaughter many of the wildlings, scattering the rest.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e9/S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png/revision/latest?cb=20150307125917" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="S04E10 - Burial of Ygritte"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png" 	data-image-name="S04E10 - Burial of Ygritte.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e9/S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150307125917"  	 width="180"  	 height="112"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e9/S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150307125917" 	 alt="S04E10 - Burial of Ygritte"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png" 	data-image-name="S04E10 - Burial of Ygritte.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="112"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:S04E10_-_Burial_of_Ygritte.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon gives Ygritte a northern burial beyond the Wall, at the request of Tormund.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon introduces himself to Stannis as <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Ned Stark</a>'s son, and suggests that Stannis arrest Mance instead of executing him, reasoning that Mance had the chance to kill him, but chose not to. Out of respect for Ned Stark, Stannis accepts, and Jon also advises Stannis to burn the bodies of the dead in order to prevent them from returning as wights. During the funeral, Jon notices <a href="/wiki/Melisandre" title="Melisandre">Melisandre</a> staring at him through the flames. Later, Jon visits Tormund, who tells Jon that Ygritte truly loved him, and asks him to lay Ygritte to rest north of the Wall. Jon later takes his love's body into the woods and burns it, weeping as he walks away.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">[40]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_5"><a href="/wiki/Season_5" title="Season 5">Season 5</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3a/Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160811101041" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Stannis on the wall"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg" 	data-image-name="Stannis on the wall.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3a/Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160811101041"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3a/Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160811101041" 	 alt="Stannis on the wall"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg" 	data-image-name="Stannis on the wall.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Stannis_on_the_wall.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon bows before Stannis.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon Snow spars with <a href="/wiki/Olly" title="Olly">Olly</a>, along with other new recruits before being summoned by <a href="/wiki/Melisandre" title="Melisandre">Melisandre</a> to see Stannis atop the Wall. He questions the Red Woman if she is cold, as she is dressed in unusually light clothing for the local climate, but she states that "the <a href="/wiki/R%27hllor" title="R'hllor">Lord's fire</a>" lives within her. Melisandre asks if Jon is a virgin. Jon replies he is not, which she approves. Jon meets with Stannis and Davos, kneeling before the king. With <a href="/wiki/Roose_Bolton" title="Roose Bolton">Roose Bolton</a> ruling Winterfell, Stannis asks Jon if he wants to avenge his fallen <a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">half-brother</a>.
</p><p>Jon reaffirms that he is a sworn brother of the Night's Watch. Davos states that his loyalty to the Watch is considered dubious because of his time spent with the wildlings. Nevertheless, Stannis wants Jon to retake <a href="/wiki/The_North" title="The North">the North</a> with the help of the wildlings, stating that he will pardon them and declare them citizens of the realm once the war is won. Stannis will give the wildlings their lives and freedom if Mance bends the knee and swears his loyalty. He gives Jon until nightfall to convince Mance, or the <a href="/wiki/King-Beyond-the-Wall" title="King-Beyond-the-Wall">King-Beyond-the-Wall</a> will be burned as a sacrifice to <a href="/wiki/R%27hllor" title="R'hllor">R'hllor</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0f/Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150413183123" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Mance wars to come"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Mance wars to come.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0f/Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413183123"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0f/Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150413183123" 	 alt="Jon and Mance wars to come"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Mance wars to come.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Mance_wars_to_come.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon attempts to convince Mance to bend the knee to Stannis.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon does his best to convince Mance to save his life as well as all the wildlings, but it is unsuccessful: the wildlings only follow him because he kneels to no one, so if he did kneel to Stannis they would lose all respect for him and ignore his commands anyway, so he might as well die with his honor intact by refusing. As Mance is led to the pyre, Stannis gives him one last chance to save his life. Mance politely refuses and is led to the stake and Melisandre lights the pyre. Unable to watch Mance suffer, Jon storms off. Just as the fire begins to fully consume Mance, he is mercifully shot through the heart with an arrow by Jon.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[41]</a></sup>
</p><p>Stannis and Davos summon Jon to discuss his future. Stannis shows him a letter delivered by <a href="/wiki/Ravens" title="Ravens">messenger-raven</a> from <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Mormont" title="Lyanna Mormont">Lyanna Mormont</a> saying she would only pledge her House to a member of <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">House Stark</a>. Stannis offers a simple solution: as king, he will officially <a href="/wiki/Legitimization" title="Legitimization">legitimize</a> Jon and make him Lord of Winterfell. Later that day the <a href="/wiki/Choosing" title="Choosing">choosing</a> for the new <a href="/wiki/Lord_Commander_of_the_Night%27s_Watch" title="Lord Commander of the Night's Watch">Lord Commander of the Night's Watch</a> has begun and many brothers of the Night's Watch have assembled to vote for either Ser Alliser Thorne (who is fervently supported by Janos) or Ser <a href="/wiki/Denys_Mallister" title="Denys Mallister">Denys Mallister</a> commander of the <a href="/wiki/The_Shadow_Tower" title="The Shadow Tower">Shadow Tower</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d6/LCJonSnow.png/revision/latest?cb=20160804232712" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="LCJonSnow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="LCJonSnow.png" 	data-image-name="LCJonSnow.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d6/LCJonSnow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160804232712"  	 width="180"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d6/LCJonSnow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160804232712" 	 alt="LCJonSnow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="LCJonSnow.png" 	data-image-name="LCJonSnow.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="91"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:LCJonSnow.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon is elected the 998th Lord Commander of the Night's Watch, fulfilling Jeor's wish.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After hearing from Jon that he intends to refuse Stannis's offer and stay true to his vows, Sam nominates Jon as the third candidate and recounts how he took command of the defense of Castle Black (including the fact that Thorne fought bravely and Janos Slynt was cowering in the pantry with Gilly) and was willing to sacrifice himself to stop Mance. With the votes cast, <a href="/wiki/Maester_Aemon" title="Maester Aemon" class="mw-redirect">Maester Aemon</a> and his aide tally the tokens and a tie is declared between Jon and Thorne. Aemon feels around in his hands for his voting chip and produces a circle token and adds it to Jon's stack amidst cheers and laughter as Jon has been chosen as the 998th Lord Commander of the Night's Watch.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[42]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon is approached by Stannis and Davos about the offer of legitimization. As the new Lord Commander, Jon reminds the king that his place is with the Night's Watch, even though his dream was to be a Stark. Stannis, a man of duty, respects his decision to keep his vow and tells Jon he intends to march on <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a> within a fortnight since the Night's Watch cannot afford to feed both his army and the wildling prisoners. He also recommends sending Alliser Thorne to command <a href="/wiki/Eastwatch-by-the-Sea" title="Eastwatch-by-the-Sea">Eastwatch-by-the-Sea</a> and that executing the wildling prisoners would be the safest choice. Stannis then leaves, but Davos stays behind and tries to further persuade Jon to help Stannis retake the North. Davos iterates that the Night's Watch is "the shield that guards the realms of men", telling Jon that it may not just mean protecting the Seven Kingdoms from beyond the Wall, but possibly taking part in battles in order to prevent the Seven Kingdoms from suffering, such as the North will under Bolton rule.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/JonSnowS5E3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160625100111" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="JonSnowS5E3"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="JonSnowS5E3.jpg" 	data-image-name="JonSnowS5E3.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/JonSnowS5E3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160625100111"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/JonSnowS5E3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160625100111" 	 alt="JonSnowS5E3"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="JonSnowS5E3.jpg" 	data-image-name="JonSnowS5E3.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:JonSnowS5E3.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lord Commander Jon Snow presides over a mess hall meeting.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During Jon's first general meeting of the garrison in the main hall as Lord Commander, he starts with some levity by assigning a black brother to oversee the digging of a new latrine pit. He also acknowledges Ser Alliser Thorne as an experienced and valuable member of the Night's Watch by naming him <a href="/wiki/First_Ranger" title="First Ranger">First Ranger</a>. Jon then orders <a href="/wiki/Janos_Slynt" title="Janos Slynt">Janos Slynt</a> to man and repair <a href="/wiki/Greyguard" title="Greyguard">Greyguard</a>, a ruined castle. Janos refuses to obey, even after Jon warns him that this was a direct order. Janos then refuses him a third time and publicly insults him, telling Jon, "You can stick your order up your bastard ass." Having publicly disobeyed and insulted Jon, the Lord Commander orders Janos taken outside, and calls for <a href="/wiki/Olly" title="Olly">Olly</a> to fetch him <a href="/wiki/Longclaw" title="Longclaw">Longclaw</a>.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/79/Small_justice_for_Ned.png/revision/latest?cb=20160730012807" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Small justice for Ned"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Small_justice_for_Ned.png" 	data-image-name="Small justice for Ned.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/79/Small_justice_for_Ned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730012807"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/79/Small_justice_for_Ned.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160730012807" 	 alt="Small justice for Ned"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Small_justice_for_Ned.png" 	data-image-name="Small justice for Ned.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Small_justice_for_Ned.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon executes Janos Slynt.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Obedience to the laws of his "father" - that the man who passes the sentence must swing the sword - Jon makes ready to personally behead Janos. While on the chopping block, Janos begins to plead for mercy, but Jon executes the cowardly former Commander of the <a href="/wiki/City_Watch" title="City Watch" class="mw-redirect">City Watch</a> with a single blow - incidentally exacting small justice on one of the men who <a href="/wiki/Massacre_in_the_Red_Keep" title="Massacre in the Red Keep">betrayed</a> Eddard to his death, and slaughtered the Stark guardsmen in the throne room and King Robert's bastard children. From across the courtyard, Stannis Baratheon sees Jon behead Janos for refusing his orders, and slightly nods in approval.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[43]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon continues to train new recruits, with Stannis, <a href="/wiki/Selyse_Florent" title="Selyse Florent" class="mw-redirect">Selyse</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shireen_Baratheon" title="Shireen Baratheon">Shireen</a>, and Melisandre observing him, with Stannis implying that he does not believe Jon to be Eddard's bastard son - saying that Eddard was always an honorable man and it wasn't in his character to randomly have sex with some tavern whore. Later, Sam presents him with requests to the Northern Lords for men for the Night's Watch.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2c/Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160809141402" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Melisandre and jon sons of the harpy"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg" 	data-image-name="Melisandre and jon sons of the harpy.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2c/Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809141402"  	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2c/Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809141402" 	 alt="Melisandre and jon sons of the harpy"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg" 	data-image-name="Melisandre and jon sons of the harpy.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="100"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Melisandre_and_jon_sons_of_the_harpy.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Melisandre attempts to seduce Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>He is reluctant to send one to Roose Bolton, <a href="/wiki/Robb_Stark" title="Robb Stark">his brother</a>'s killer, until Sam convinces him that they must stay neutral and ask for as many men as they can for the Watch, and right now the Boltons rule the North and have the most men - leading Jon to sign the request angrily. Melisandre enters his office and again tries to persuade him to chase <a href="/wiki/Roose_Bolton" title="Roose Bolton">the</a> <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_Bolton" title="Ramsay Bolton">rats</a> out of his home, but he claims that Castle Black is now his home. She attempts to seduce him, sensing a power inside his blood, but Jon rebuffs her, remembering his love for Ygritte. As Melisandre leaves, she tells him, "You know nothing, Jon Snow".<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[44]</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, Jon consults Maester <a href="/wiki/Aemon" title="Aemon">Aemon</a> for advice on a hard decision he is about to make, noting that half the men in the Night's Watch despise him for his sympathy for the wildlings, but Aemon tells him to "Kill the boy, and let the man be born," in other words, just make the hard choice and do what he believes is best. Indeed, Jon's plan is to allow the wildlings to pass the Wall and settle in the North as subjects of the Seven Kingdoms or even let them join the Watch. Jon's idea is met with harsh criticism, even from his closest friends such as Edd and Olly, but Jon's goal is actually to keep the wildlings from falling into the hands of the coming White Walker army. Jon points out that every single wildling left on the north side of the Wall will be killed, then resurrected and added to the White Walkers ever-growing army of the undead.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/18/Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150525133127" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Kill the Boy promo"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="Kill the Boy promo.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/18/Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150525133127"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/18/Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150525133127" 	 alt="Kill the Boy promo"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="Kill the Boy promo.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kill_the_Boy_promo.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon watches as Stannis leaves Castle Black.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon speaks alone with Tormund, who reveals that the remainder of Mance's army probably fled back to <a href="/wiki/Hardhome" title="Hardhome">Hardhome</a>, a large fishing village on the coast. Jon requests that Tormund go there and negotiate with the remaining wildling chieftains, to let them pass through the Wall on Jon's terms. Tormund agrees, so long as Jon accompanies him so that the wildlings will know it is not a trap. Jon borrows several of Stannis's ships for the journey (as he is marching inland and won't be using them). Later, as Stannis prepares to leave Castle Black for Winterfell with his army, Jon thanks him for his help, promises him he will have his ships back, and watches Stannis depart for Winterfell to take his childhood home back from the Boltons.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[45]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon later prepares to leave Castle Black with Tormund and a group of black brothers including Edd. He entrusts the care of the Night's Watch to Thorne, who criticizes his mission, and says his farewells to Sam, who gives him a bag of <a href="/wiki/Dragonglass" title="Dragonglass">dragonglass</a> daggers in case he should run into White Walkers on the way. He hugs Sam for what might be the last time and leaves Castle Black on his mission.
</p><p>Later at Winterfell, Ramsay Bolton mentions to Sansa Stark that Jon has been made the new Lord Commander of the Night's Watch, citing Jon as an example of a bastard who rose high in the world, claiming that if Jon did it, then so can he.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">[46]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/91/Hardhome-boat.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150528185140" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Hardhome-boat"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Hardhome-boat.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hardhome-boat.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/91/Hardhome-boat.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150528185140"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/91/Hardhome-boat.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150528185140" 	 alt="Hardhome-boat"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Hardhome-boat.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hardhome-boat.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hardhome-boat.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon arrives at Hardhome, eager to evacuate the wildlings.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon reaches Hardhome with his companions. After Tormund kills the <a href="/wiki/Lord_of_Bones" title="Lord of Bones">Lord of Bones</a> for challenging him, he and Jon go inside a hut to speak with the leaders of the clans. Though the wildlings are prepared to kill Jon for murdering Mance, Tormund stands up for him and reveals that Jon, in fact, killed Mance out of mercy. Jon offers to share the dragonglass weapons with the wildlings and allow them to settle on land south of the Wall, if they promise to aid the Night's Watch in the coming battle against the White Walkers: even if they and all the men of the Seven Kingdoms are not enough to stop them, they can at least die fighting. Five thousand wildlings agree while the rest decide to stay, though Tormund hopes more will come around with time.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/23/JonSnowHardhome.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160604042246" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="JonSnowHardhome"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="JonSnowHardhome.jpg" 	data-image-name="JonSnowHardhome.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/23/JonSnowHardhome.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160604042246"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/23/JonSnowHardhome.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160604042246" 	 alt="JonSnowHardhome"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="JonSnowHardhome.jpg" 	data-image-name="JonSnowHardhome.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:JonSnowHardhome.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon uses Longclaw to defeat a White Walker.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, as they are preparing to leave, they are all attacked by an army of wights. Jon fights his way to the hut to retrieve the dragonglass daggers, but he is ambushed by a White Walker. They fight for a while and Jon is almost killed until he retrieves Longclaw. To the surprise of both Jon and the White Walker, Longclaw doesn't shatter from the cold of the Walker's weapon when he uses it to parry his attack - because it is made of <a href="/wiki/Valyrian_steel" title="Valyrian steel">Valyrian steel</a>, forged with <a href="/wiki/Dragons" title="Dragons">dragon-fire</a> and spells. Jon quickly regains his ground and slashes the White Walker with it, making it shatter into a cloud of ice particles, and revealing that the White Walkers can also be killed by Valyrian steel.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e1/Hardhome-0.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160604043057" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Hardhome-0"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Hardhome-0.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hardhome-0.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e1/Hardhome-0.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160604043057"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e1/Hardhome-0.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160604043057" 	 alt="Hardhome-0"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Hardhome-0.jpg" 	data-image-name="Hardhome-0.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hardhome-0.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon gazes upon the horrific aftermath of the Hardhome massacre.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Edd helps Jon to his feet and they make it back to the boats to Stannis's ships, with the wights refusing to follow them in the water. But as they leave, the <a href="/wiki/The_Night%27s_King" title="The Night's King" class="mw-redirect">Night's King</a> himself appears at thousands of e wharf and shares a long glance with Jon, at the same time using his magic to raise all of the dead as wights before Jon's eyes. Jon looks on in obvious terror, as he knows the slaughter he just witnessed is merely a prelude to what is coming for all of Westeros.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/eb/Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150604205147" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Samwell The Dance of Dragons"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Samwell The Dance of Dragons.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/eb/Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150604205147"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/eb/Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150604205147" 	 alt="Jon and Samwell The Dance of Dragons"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Samwell The Dance of Dragons.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Samwell_The_Dance_of_Dragons.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sam and Jon watch as the wildlings exodus.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and the others make it back to the north side of <a href="/wiki/Castle_Black" title="Castle Black">Castle Black</a> on foot and he makes himself seen by Alliser Thorne so that they will be let inside. Thorne hesitates but ultimately relents and orders the gates to be opened. As the wildlings are let through Castle Black into the Seven Kingdoms, Jon laments not being able to save the rest, while Samwell comforts him, reminding him that he at least saved a few, who would have died too if he did nothing. Thorne, however, warns Jon, telling him that his kind heart will get him killed. Indeed, as Jon looks around, he sees almost all of his brothers looking at him scornfully, among them <a href="/wiki/Olly" title="Olly">Olly</a>, <a href="/wiki/Othell_Yarwyck" title="Othell Yarwyck">Othell Yarwyck</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bowen_Marsh" title="Bowen Marsh">Bowen Marsh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[48]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150611144059" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Mothers Mercy 04"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg" 	data-image-name="Mothers Mercy 04.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150611144059"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/1a/Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150611144059" 	 alt="Mothers Mercy 04"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg" 	data-image-name="Mothers Mercy 04.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mother%E2%80%99s_Mercy_04.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon agrees to send Sam to Oldtown.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon discusses with Sam the war against the White Walkers, and his increasingly strained relationship with the rest of the Night's Watch. Sam asks for leave to take <a href="/wiki/Gilly" title="Gilly">Gilly</a> and her baby with him to <a href="/wiki/Oldtown" title="Oldtown">Oldtown</a> where he will train to become a maester. Sam reasons that he is better suited to the life of a maester than a warrior, and that the Night's Watch needs to fill the gap left by the late Aemon Targaryen. Jon is reluctant, as he has few friends nowadays, and also points out that as a maester, Sam's vow of chastity will be doubly prevalent, before finding out that Sam and Gilly have had sex already (to Jon's amusement). Jon eventually agrees to Sam's request and sees him off.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Davos_Seaworth" title="Davos Seaworth">Davos Seaworth</a> returns to Castle Black to beg Jon for soldiers - though this was really just a ruse to get Davos out of Stannis's camp, because he had become so desperate that he gave in to <a href="/wiki/Melisandre" title="Melisandre">Melisandre</a>'s request to burn Shireen as a sacrifice.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150615200645" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Davos and Jon hear about the deaths of Stannis and Shireen"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg" 	data-image-name="Davos and Jon hear about the deaths of Stannis and Shireen.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150615200645"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/89/Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150615200645" 	 alt="Davos and Jon hear about the deaths of Stannis and Shireen"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg" 	data-image-name="Davos and Jon hear about the deaths of Stannis and Shireen.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Davos_and_Jon_hear_about_the_deaths_of_Stannis_and_Shireen.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Davos are heartbroken with the deaths of Shireen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon points out that the Night's Watch, even if they do ally with Stannis, will not be enough, and the wildlings will not fight for Stannis as it isn't their fight. Their argument is broken up by the arrival of a wearied and addled Melisandre - who abandoned Stannis when it became apparent he would lose the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Winterfell" title="Battle of Winterfell" class="mw-redirect">Battle of Winterfell</a>. When Davos questions her about Stannis and Shireen, she says nothing yet her sorrow is manifest, all but confirming the demise of his king and princess. Still forlorn and at a loss for words, Melisandre heads inside the castle, leaving both Jon and Davos horrified at the news.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f5/Jon%27s_death.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150713173939" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon&amp;#039;s death"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon%27s_death.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon&#39;s death.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f5/Jon%27s_death.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150713173939"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f5/Jon%27s_death.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150713173939" 	 alt="Jon&amp;#039;s death"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon%27s_death.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon&#39;s death.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon%27s_death.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">After being stabbed by his own men, Jon dies.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>That night while reading messages, Olly comes to Jon and tells him one of the wildlings knows of the whereabouts of his uncle <a href="/wiki/Benjen_Stark" title="Benjen Stark">Benjen Stark</a>, who has been missing since before the Great Ranging. Jon quickly follows Thorne to a gathering of his Watch brothers, only to find a sign marked "Traitor". Thorne, Yarwyck, Marsh and two other black brothers <a href="/wiki/Mutiny_at_Castle_Black" title="Mutiny at Castle Black">proceed to stab</a> Jon while uttering, "For the Watch." As the wounded Jon kneels, gasping for breath, Olly tearfully comes forward and after a few moments of pause, stabs Jon in the heart and declares, "For the Watch." Jon collapses and dies from his wounds before the mutineers leave him out in the cold to bleed out.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[49]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_6"><a href="/wiki/Season_6" title="Season 6">Season 6</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/The_Red_Woman_17.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160503012008" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="The Red Woman 17"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="The_Red_Woman_17.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Red Woman 17.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/The_Red_Woman_17.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160503012008"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/d8/The_Red_Woman_17.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160503012008" 	 alt="The Red Woman 17"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="The_Red_Woman_17.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Red Woman 17.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Red_Woman_17.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Edd mourns over Jon's corpse, realizing that Thorne was the orchestrator of Jon's demise.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon seeing the body of his dead master, <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">Ghost</a> howls in mourning from his pen. His cries summon Davos, Edd and a handful of other black brothers who quickly move Jon's body to his quarters. They quickly realize that Thorne was most likely the orchestrator of Jon's demise, and free Ghost to help them protect Jon's body while Edd leaves to find Tormund and the Wildlings. Melisandre also looks at Jon's body and claims that she had seen a vision of him fighting at Winterfell, though Davos remains adamant that Jon is gone for good. Thorne later approaches Davos and the loyal brothers with a promise of amnesty if they throw their weapons down and surrender, though they refuse to back down, despite Thorne's threats of death if they don't.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[50]</a></sup>
</p>
