<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a5/Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160502032414" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon Snow Alive"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Snow Alive.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a5/Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160502032414"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/a/a5/Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160502032414" 	 alt="Jon Snow Alive"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Snow Alive.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_Snow_Alive.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon awakens after being resurrected by Melisandre.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>After being rescued by Edd and the wildlings, Davos goes to Melisandre and asks if there's any magic she knows of that can resurrect Jon. Shaken by Stannis' death, she says all she believed in was a lie. Davos states that he wasn't asking the R'hllor for help, but Melisandre herself. Melisandre then performs a ritual with Jon's body: cleaning his wounds, cutting some of his hair, trimming his beard, and burning it in the fire, all while chanting in <a href="/wiki/High_Valyrian" title="High Valyrian">High Valyrian</a>. Her attempts seem to be in vain.<a href="/wiki/Tormund" title="Tormund">Tormund</a> storms out in frustration, those remaining leave the room one by one, and after a few moments alone with Ghost, Jon awakens, gasping for air.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[51]</a></sup>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/Oathbreaker_18.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160512164233" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Oathbreaker 18"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Oathbreaker_18.jpg" 	data-image-name="Oathbreaker 18.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/Oathbreaker_18.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512164233"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/Oathbreaker_18.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160512164233" 	 alt="Oathbreaker 18"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Oathbreaker_18.jpg" 	data-image-name="Oathbreaker 18.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Oathbreaker_18.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon is questioned on the afterlife.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Coming back to his senses, Jon is accosted by Davos and Melisandre. He reflects on his perceived failure in spite of doing the right thing, but after some encouragement from Davos, Jon gets dressed and enters the courtyard to the surprise of every wildling present, reuniting with Tormund and Edd. Later, the leaders of the mutiny are rounded up for execution. After hearing last words from each (with the exception of Olly), Jon once again acts in accordance with his father's law that "the man who passes the sentence should swing the sword" and personally cuts the trapdoor rope, hanging them simultaneously.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/dd/Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png/revision/latest?cb=20160509224337" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Screen Shot 2016-05-09 at 5.42.20 PM"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png" 	data-image-name="Screen Shot 2016-05-09 at 5.42.20 PM.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/dd/Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160509224337"  	 width="180"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/d/dd/Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160509224337" 	 alt="Screen Shot 2016-05-09 at 5.42.20 PM"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png" 	data-image-name="Screen Shot 2016-05-09 at 5.42.20 PM.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="105"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Screen_Shot_2016-05-09_at_5.42.20_PM.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon relinquishes his command to Edd.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Technically free from his vows, Jon then passes his cloak and command to Edd, declaring his intent to leave the Night's Watch.<sup id="cite_ref-E53_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E53-2">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f3/Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160516164908" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Book of the Stranger 36"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg" 	data-image-name="Book of the Stranger 36.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f3/Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160516164908"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f3/Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160516164908" 	 alt="Book of the Stranger 36"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg" 	data-image-name="Book of the Stranger 36.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Book_of_the_Stranger_36.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon reunites with Sansa.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A day later, Jon packs his belongings. Edd chastises him for abandoning the Night's Watch despite the threat of the White Walkers looming, and reminds Jon of the oath he swore. Jon retorts by saying that he already died, and that he couldn't stay after what was done to him. His half-sister, Sansa Stark arrives after escaping <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_Bolton" title="Ramsay Bolton">Ramsay Bolton</a> with help from Theon Greyjoy, along with <a href="/wiki/Brienne_of_Tarth" title="Brienne of Tarth">Brienne of Tarth</a> and <a href="/wiki/Podrick_Payne" title="Podrick Payne">Podrick Payne</a>. After a moment of stunned disbelief, Jon joyfully embraces his long-lost sibling. Shortly thereafter, Jon brings Sansa inside to get warm and eat. The two share their lives since leaving Winterfell, and reminisce about their childhoods. Sansa regretfully mentions how awful she was to Jon during their youth, and that she felt guilty about it for years. Jon shrugs it off as childhood mischief, though he forgives Sansa after she presses the issue. The pair acknowledge that their last haven is Winterfell, and even then, the Boltons are currently occupying it, but Jon is reluctant to fight again after everything he's been through.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0d/Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160516164909" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Book of the Stranger 35"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg" 	data-image-name="Book of the Stranger 35.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0d/Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160516164909"  	 width="180"  	 height="118"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0d/Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160516164909" 	 alt="Book of the Stranger 35"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg" 	data-image-name="Book of the Stranger 35.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="118"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Book_of_the_Stranger_35.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon receives a threatening letter from Ramsay Bolton.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, as Jon eats with Sansa, Brienne, Podrick, Tormund, and Edd, he receives a <a href="/wiki/Bastard_letter" title="Bastard letter">letter</a> from Ramsay, informing him that he is holding Rickon prisoner and furiously demanding the return of Sansa on threat of massacring Jon's allies, raping Sansa and murdering Rickon and Jon. Jon notes Ramsay's signature and Sansa deduces that <a href="/wiki/Roose_Bolton" title="Roose Bolton">Roose Bolton</a> is dead. Jon asks Tormund how many men he has; Tormund says 2,000, not enough to fight Ramsay's 5,000 by themselves. With some urging from Sansa to rally the Northern Houses still loyal to the Starks, Jon resolves to take Ramsay down.<sup id="cite_ref-E54_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E54-9">[10]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2d/The_Door_34.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160808075202" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="The Door 34"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="The_Door_34.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Door 34.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2d/The_Door_34.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160808075202"  	 width="180"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/2d/The_Door_34.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160808075202" 	 alt="The Door 34"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="The_Door_34.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Door 34.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="117"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Door_34.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon plans his strategy against Ramsay.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While discussing strategy with Davos, Melisandre, Sansa, Brienne, Edd, and Tormund, Jon bitterly notes that they simply don't have the numbers to challenge the Boltons at present. Even though the three most powerful houses are already backing the Boltons, Jon suggests rallying the weaker houses, as their combined strength would give them a numerical advantage when combined with his current forces. When Sansa mentions Brynden Tully's recapture of Riverrun and the virtual guarantee of support from the Tullys, Jon is surprised that Sansa has such valuable information. Thereafter, Jon, Sansa, Tormund and Brienne leave Castle Black.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[52]</a></sup>
</p><p>With help from Tormund, Jon speaks with the wildlings and asks for their help in the coming battle against Ramsay. Though Tormund stands by Jon, Dalba is skeptical, citing that they were allowed into the North to help fight against the White Walkers, not the Boltons. Jon agrees this isn't their fight and he shouldn't be asking for their help but points out that if Ramsay wins, he will wipe them all out anyway. Tormund speaks up for Jon, saying he died for the wildlings' well-being and if they don't help him, they are "cowards". The wildlings agree after Wun Wun stands up and says "Snow", confirming his allegiance. Jon, Sansa, and Davos later accost Lady <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Mormont" title="Lyanna Mormont">Lyanna Mormont</a>, who previously refused to aid Stannis Baratheon. Jon tells Lyanna of his friendship and service under her uncle, Jeor Mormont, while he was in the Night's Watch, though Lyanna initially refuses them, citing that Jon is a bastard and Sansa has been married into House Lannister and House Bolton. Jon reveals that Ramsay is holding Rickon hostage, and Davos manages to convince her that they need to defeat Ramsay in order to unite the North against the coming White Walkers. Lyanna agrees and supplies them with sixty-two men, the remaining force of House Mormont, promising that each will fight with the worth of ten men.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170830232538" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="607 Jon Robett Promo"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="607 Jon Robett Promo.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170830232538"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/53/607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170830232538" 	 alt="607 Jon Robett Promo"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg" 	data-image-name="607 Jon Robett Promo.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:607_Jon_Robett_Promo.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon fails to recruit Robett.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, Jon fails to convince <a href="/wiki/Robett_Glover" title="Robett Glover">Robett Glover</a> to pledge his allegiance to them, as he cites Robb Stark's failures to protect the North from the Ironborn and Jon's allegiance with the wildlings. Despite being heavily outnumbered, Jon remains adamant that they attack Winterfell before Ramsay gathers more men or the weather turns against them. Behind Jon's back, however, Sansa sends a letter calling for help.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[53]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160615184848" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 03"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 03.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160615184848"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3e/Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160615184848" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 03"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 03.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Bastards_03.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Sansa attend a swift consultation with Ramsay.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ramsay, <a href="/wiki/Smalljon_Umber" title="Smalljon Umber">Smalljon Umber</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Harald_Karstark" title="Harald Karstark">Harald Karstark</a> meet with Jon, Sansa, Tormund, Davos, and Lyanna at the battlefield the day before the battle. Jon offers Ramsay a chance to settle their dispute in one on one combat but Ramsay refuses, citing his almost certain victory due to his significantly larger army. Ramsay offers surrender terms saying he will pardon Jon for breaking his Night's Watch vows if he will hand Sansa over, which is ignored. Sansa asks for proof of Rickon's capture, which he provides by way of the decapitated head of his direwolf, Shaggydog. Sansa refuses the terms of surrender and tells Ramsay he will die the following day before riding off.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/49/Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170826015409" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 16"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 16.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/49/Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170826015409"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/49/Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170826015409" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 16"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 16.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Bastards_16.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sansa criticizes Jon's underestimation of Ramsay.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon holds a meeting with Tormund and Davos, in which he discusses their battle plan to let the Boltons attack the middle of their formation in order to encircle their army. After the meeting, Sansa criticizes Jon for not listening to her advice and for attacking too early, insisting they need more men. Jon responds that this is the largest army they could possibly gather. Jon meets with Melisandre and insists to her not to bring him back if he should fall in the battle. Melisandre insists it's not her gift that has brought Jon back but the Lord of Light's and that only the Lord of Light can decide Jon's fate.<sup id="cite_ref-E59_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E59-53">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b4/Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160621185655" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 46"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 46.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b4/Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185655"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/b/b4/Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185655" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 46"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 46.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Bastards_46.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon attempts to save Rickon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The armies gather the following morning as Ramsay brings out Rickon. Telling Rickon that they are playing a game, he tells Rickon to run towards Jon and as Rickon does so, Ramsay brings out a bow. Jon desperately rides out on a horse to try to save Rickon as Ramsay fires arrows at him. Ramsay appears to have no intention of hitting Rickon with his few shots but eventually, just as Jon is about to reach his brother, Rickon is struck in the back with an arrow and killed.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/22/Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160620164817" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the bastards Jon main"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the bastards Jon main.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/22/Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160620164817"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/22/Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160620164817" 	 alt="Battle of the bastards Jon main"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the bastards Jon main.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_bastards_Jon_main.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon Snow fights against the Bolton army.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Jon now defenseless in the middle of the battlefield and charging the Bolton cavalry alone, Bolton archers fire volleys of arrows in his direction. Davos commands the Stark cavalry to follow their commander and they begin their charge to meet the Bolton cavalry, narrowly saving Jon from being trampled and forcing them to abandon their initial strategy of luring the Bolton army into encirclement. After luring Jon's army forwards, Ramsay executes his own pincer movement with his infantry, completely encircling the Stark/Wildling army. The Bolton army continues to press their advantage, with interlocking spears from all directions forcing Jon's army closer and closer together.
</p><p>Jon nearly suffocates as he is pushed beneath the tide of Wildlings that are pushed into one another, but he eventually claws his way out, just in time to see Petyr Baelish and Sansa arrive with reinforcements courtesy of House Arryn. The cavalry from the Vale quickly flanks the encircling Bolton army, which is decimated. Vindicated, Jon makes eye contact with Ramsay as he retreats from the battlefield, clearly satisfied by this turn of events and realizing that Sansa was right all along. Ramsay returns to Winterfell and closes the gates, confident that their opponent is not equipped for a siege of Winterfell, as long as they remain within the gates, and he readies his archers.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160621185502" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 39"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 39.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185502"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/21/Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185502" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 39"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 39.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Bastards_39.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A bloodied Jon confronts Ramsay.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>However, unexpectedly, with the help of the giant Wun Weg Wun Dar Wun, Jon's forces manage to breach the gates, and the remaining Bolton forces are defeated, although Wun Wun is severely injured by a barrage of arrows and spears, and eventually succumbs to Ramsay's final arrow, as Jon and Tormund watch on in horror, helpless to save their friend.<sup id="cite_ref-E59_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E59-53">[54]</a></sup> Ramsay finally accepts Jon's offer to a one-on-one duel, while wielding a bow and arrow. Grabbing a nearby shield, Jon deftly blocks all of Ramsay's shots with it until he gets close enough to smack the bow out of Ramsay's hands and hit him to the ground, whereupon he furiously punches Ramsay's face into a bloody pulp.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c9/Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160621185500" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 41"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 41.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c9/Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185500"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c9/Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621185500" 	 alt="Battle of the Bastards 41"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg" 	data-image-name="Battle of the Bastards 41.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Battle_of_the_Bastards_41.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon orders Rickon's burial.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though it seems as if Jon will kill Ramsay, he stops when he sees Sansa, knowing she has as much right to revenge as he does. Jon orders Ramsay locked up and the remaining Boltons surrender, restoring House Stark's hold on Winterfell. Rickon's body is found and Jon orders his body buried in the crypt with Ned's bones. Sansa asks Jon for Ramsay's whereabouts, and he directs her to the kennels, where she kills Ramsay that night by setting his own <a href="/wiki/Bastard%27s_girls" title="Bastard's girls">hounds</a> on him.<sup id="cite_ref-E59_53-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E59-53">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160809031624" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="The Winds of Winter 20"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Winds of Winter 20.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809031624"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/7/70/The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809031624" 	 alt="The Winds of Winter 20"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Winds of Winter 20.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Winds_of_Winter_20.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon banishes Melisandre.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the aftermath, in the Great Hall with Melisandre, Jon reminisces about how his family sat at the main table during feasts while he was mostly made to sit away with the squires (or sometimes to remain outside in the case of Robert Baratheon's visit), though they both agree that Jon was luckier than most bastard children. Davos then enters and openly accuses Melisandre of sacrificing Shireen, which Melisandre admits, though also pointing out that her magic still brought Jon back to life. Shocked at the revelation, Jon orders Melisandre to leave the North on threat of execution.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/26/Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160621224948" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Winds of winter jon snow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Winds of winter jon snow.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/26/Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621224948"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/2/26/Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160621224948" 	 alt="Winds of winter jon snow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Winds of winter jon snow.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Winds_of_winter_jon_snow.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Sansa discuss the arrival of winter.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Jon watches Melisandre riding away from the top of the castle's walls, he tells Sansa that the lord's chambers are being prepared for her and when Sansa tries to say Jon should have them, Jon says, as a bastard, he's not "a Stark" and that Sansa is the Lady of Winterfell. Jon continues that the battle was won because she brought the Knights of the Vale. Sansa apologizes for not telling him about the Vale army and when Jon asks her about Littlefinger, Sansa says he is not trustworthy. Jon responds he and Sansa must trust each other completely now and kisses her on the forehead. Sansa informs him that a <i>white</i> <a href="/wiki/Ravens" title="Ravens">messenger-raven</a> has just arrived from <a href="/wiki/The_Citadel" title="The Citadel">the Citadel</a>, officially announcing that the years-long autumn is over, and winter has <i>come</i> - which many fear will be as long as the ten-year summer which preceded it. Jon wryly points out that their father always promised it would come some day.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160809103733" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="The Winds of Winter 11"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Winds of Winter 11.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809103733"  	 width="180"  	 height="271"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/60/The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160809103733" 	 alt="The Winds of Winter 11"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg" 	data-image-name="The Winds of Winter 11.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="271"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Winds_of_Winter_11.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon intently listens to Lyanna's rhetoric.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Some time later, the surviving heads of all the Northern vassal Houses convene in Winterfell's great hall, along with the lords of the Vale who came to their rescue with their large army (such as <a href="/wiki/Yohn_Royce" title="Yohn Royce">Yohn Royce</a> and Littlefinger). They debate what to do next. Lyanna Mormont rises and shames those who did not join Jon and Sansa to help defeat Ramsay. She reiterates that the North knows no king but the <a href="/wiki/King_in_the_North" title="King in the North">King in the North</a>, whose name is "Stark." Lyanna continues by saying that <i>Jon</i> may be a bastard but she doesn't care and he is a Stark to her. She hails Jon as the new King in the North. <a href="/wiki/Wyman_Manderly" title="Wyman Manderly">Wyman Manderly</a>, whose son <a href="/wiki/Wendel_Manderly" title="Wendel Manderly">Wendel</a> was killed at the Red Wedding, also rises to apologize, saying he didn't send aid before because he didn't want to send his men to die for nothing, but now Jon has avenged the Red Wedding.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f0/Jon_Snow_is_declared_King_in_The_North_Season_6_Episode_10_Preview..jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160627155634" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon Snow is declared King in The North Season 6 Episode 10 Preview."  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Snow_is_declared_King_in_The_North_Season_6_Episode_10_Preview..jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Snow is declared King in The North Season 6 Episode 10 Preview..jpg"
