 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/f0/Jon_Snow_is_declared_King_in_The_North_Season_6_Episode_10_Preview..jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160627155634" 	 alt="Jon Snow is declared King in The North Season 6 Episode 10 Preview."  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Snow_is_declared_King_in_The_North_Season_6_Episode_10_Preview..jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Snow is declared King in The North Season 6 Episode 10 Preview..jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_Snow_is_declared_King_in_The_North_Season_6_Episode_10_Preview..jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon Snow is hailed as the new King in the North, the White Wolf.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>Lord Wyman goes on to call Jon "the White Wolf" and he too proclaims him King. <a href="/wiki/Robett_Glover" title="Robett Glover">Robett Glover</a> apologizes profusely, saying that he dishonored himself by not aiding him before, and he only didn't help Jon because he thought he had no hope of winning. Lord <a href="/wiki/Cley_Cerwyn" title="Cley Cerwyn">Cerwyn</a>, whose parents were flayed alive by Ramsay Bolton and did not help out of fear, also swears his allegiance. All of the gathered lords of the North and the Vale draw and raise their swords and hail Jon as the new King in the North, echoing how Robb Stark's bannermen previously proclaimed him king. Surprised, Jon shares a look with Sansa, who returns Jon's smile as he stands. However, Sansa's smile vanishes when she sees Littlefinger glowering in the corner of the hall.
<p>Meanwhile, beyond the Wall, Bran experiences a vision about Jon's origins and realizes he is actually the son of Rhaegar Targaryen and Lyanna Stark.<sup id="cite_ref-E60_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E60-3">[4]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_7"><a href="/wiki/Season_7" title="Season 7">Season 7</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/57/GOT_Season_7_05.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170612172522" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="GOT Season 7 05"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="GOT_Season_7_05.jpg" 	data-image-name="GOT Season 7 05.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/57/GOT_Season_7_05.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172522"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/5/57/GOT_Season_7_05.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170612172522" 	 alt="GOT Season 7 05"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="GOT_Season_7_05.jpg" 	data-image-name="GOT Season 7 05.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:GOT_Season_7_05.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon at a meeting at Winterfell.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To prepare for the forthcoming conflict with the Night King, the newly declared King Jon orders his bannermen to conscript all able-bodied men and boys aged 10 to 60 for combat training. However, he notes that having only half of the population in the North fighting the White Walkers is not enough he also orders that every woman and girl should also be trained and equipped as well. He also asks that all maesters should start searching for dragonglass. He stresses that dragonglass is now more valuable than gold due to the threat of the White Walkers.
</p><p>When Sansa advocates that the Umbers and Karstarks be stripped of their lands and titles as punishment for supporting Ramsay Bolton, Jon advocates forgiveness and insists that children will not be punished for the crimes of their fathers. Despite Sansa's continued insistence, Jon insists his decision is final and summons Ned Umber and Alys Karstark to reaffirm their loyalty to House Stark. They oblige and kneel before King Jon. Jon says that the mistakes of the past don't matter anymore.
</p><p>In private, Jon Snow chides Sansa for questioning his decision-making in front of the other lords and ladies and tells her to trust him. When Sansa reminds him that the late Joffrey Baratheon did not tolerate dissent, Jon reassures her that he is not Joffrey. Sansa tells Jon that she knows he is nothing like Joffrey and assures Jon that he is good at leadership but she stresses that he must act wiser than Ned and Robb.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[55]</a></sup>
</p><p>At <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a>, Jon, Sansa, and Davos discuss Tyrion's letter that they have received. While Sansa suspects it might be a trap, Jon doesn't think so due to Tyrion ending the letter with the line "<i>all dwarfs are bastards in their fathers' eyes</i>", which Tyrion has told Jon in their first meeting years ago. Even so, Jon agrees that now is not the right time to go to Dragonstone. Davos opines that Dany will make a good ally in the war to come against the <a href="/wiki/White_Walkers" title="White Walkers">White Walkers</a>.
</p><p>Later Jon receives a raven from Sam informing him of his discovery of dragonglass on Dragonstone. At another gathering of the Northern lords Jon informs them of Sam's discovery and Daenerys's invitation telling them that he has decided to accept. Many of the Lords, including Sansa, openly disapprove, but Jon stresses that they need both the dragonglass and powerful allies like Daenerys to have any chance at defeating the Night King. He names Sansa as Regent to rule in his place until he returns.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6d/Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170715162419" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon Petyr Winterfell Crypt"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Petyr Winterfell Crypt.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6d/Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170715162419"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/6/6d/Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170715162419" 	 alt="Jon Petyr Winterfell Crypt"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon Petyr Winterfell Crypt.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_Petyr_Winterfell_Crypt.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon sees through Petyr's manipulation.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the crypts beneath Winterfell Jon pays respects to Ned until he is interrupted by Littlefinger. Littlefinger tries to sweet talk Jon, but he sees through his manipulation and starts to walk away. Littlefinger informs Jon of his love for Sansa, which causes him to lose his temper and start to strangle him. Jon threatens Littlefinger saying that he will kill him if he ever touches Sansa. He then leaves the crypt and gives a farewell nod to Sansa before joining Davos on the ride to White Harbor, where they will take a ship to Dragonstone.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e7/Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170729193447" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Davos on Dragonstone"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Davos on Dragonstone.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e7/Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170729193447"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/e7/Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170729193447" 	 alt="Jon and Davos on Dragonstone"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Davos on Dragonstone.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Davos_on_Dragonstone.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Davos arrive on Dragonstone.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon and Davos arrive at <a href="/wiki/Dragonstone_(island)" title="Dragonstone (island)">Dragonstone</a>, and are immediately greeted by Tyrion and <a href="/wiki/Missandei" title="Missandei">Missandei</a>. Upon meeting, Tyrion address Jon as the <a href="/wiki/Bastardy" title="Bastardy">bastard</a> of <a href="/wiki/Winterfell" title="Winterfell">Winterfell</a> while Jon addressed him as the "dwarf" of <a href="/wiki/Casterly_Rock" title="Casterly Rock">Casterly Rock</a>. Jon observes that Tyrion has picked up some scars. Jon also introduces Davos while Tyrion introduces Missandei, who requests that they surrender their weapons. Jon and his entourage hand over their weapons to <a href="/wiki/Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Daenerys Targaryen">Daenerys Targaryen</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dothraki" title="Dothraki">Dothraki</a> guards.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[56]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3b/Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731203317" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Walk to Dragonstone TQJ"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Walk to Dragonstone TQJ.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3b/Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203317"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3b/Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203317" 	 alt="Walk to Dragonstone TQJ"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Walk to Dragonstone TQJ.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Walk_to_Dragonstone_TQJ.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Davos and Jon first lay eyes on Queen Daenerys Targaryen's dragons.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the walk to the <a href="/wiki/Dragonstone_(castle)" title="Dragonstone (castle)">castle</a>, Missandei walks with Davos and tells him that she comes from the island of <a href="/wiki/Naath" title="Naath">Naath</a>. Davos remarks that it was a paradise full of palm trees. Jon and Tyrion talk about Sansa's marriage to Tyrion. Tyrion assures Jon that it was a sham and remarks that she is a lot smarter than she lets on, which Jon agrees. While Jon is aware about the fate of the previous <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">Starks</a> who had met with the <a href="/wiki/Aerys_II_Targaryen" title="Aerys II Targaryen">Mad King</a>, Jon insists that he is not a Stark. Jon and Davos are startled at the sight of <a href="/wiki/Drogon" title="Drogon">Drogon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rhaegal" title="Rhaegal">Rhaegal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Viserion" title="Viserion">Viserion</a> flying low over the causeway and dive to the ground, while an amused Missandei and Tyrion retain their composure. Offering Jon a hand up, Tyrion says he wishes he could tell Jon he'll get used to the dragons  but no one is quite used to them except their mother, who is waiting for Jon within.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3c/Jon_StarkSnow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170729193011" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon StarkSnow"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_StarkSnow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon StarkSnow.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3c/Jon_StarkSnow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170729193011"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/3c/Jon_StarkSnow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170729193011" 	 alt="Jon StarkSnow"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_StarkSnow.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon StarkSnow.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_StarkSnow.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon clasps eyes on the Dragon Queen.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the throne room, Missandei introduces Queen Daenerys's many titles while Davos introduces Jon Snow simply as <a href="/wiki/King_in_the_North" title="King in the North">King in the North</a>. Daenerys thanks Jon for traveling so far but insists that he is a mere Lord. Davos begs to differ but Daenerys responds that there has been no King in the North ever since <a href="/wiki/Torrhen_Stark" title="Torrhen Stark">Torrhen Stark</a> bent the knee to <a href="/wiki/Aegon_the_Conqueror" title="Aegon the Conqueror" class="mw-redirect">Aegon the Conqueror</a> and adds that an oath lasts for perpetuity. Dany then reiterates her demand for Jon to bend the knee but he refuses. When Dany accuses him of breaking faith with <a href="/wiki/House_Targaryen" title="House Targaryen">House Targaryen</a>, Jon reminds her that the Mad King burnt his grandfather <a href="/wiki/Rickard_Stark" title="Rickard Stark">Rickard</a> and uncle <a href="/wiki/Brandon_Stark_(son_of_Rickard)" title="Brandon Stark (son of Rickard)">Brandon</a>.
</p><p>Daenerys apologizes for her father's actions and stresses that children should not be punished for the crimes of their parents. She then urges Jon to renew the historic allegiance between their two great houses. Jon expresses agreement with Daenerys's view that children should not be punished for the crimes of their parents but argues that he is not beholden to his ancestors' oaths. Jon tells her that he has come for her help. Dany reminds him that she has three dragons and Dothraki who have pledged themselves to her. Getting to the point of his trip, Jon likens the fighting between the Great Houses to children squabbling over a game. Jon Snow points out that the Army of the Dead is their true enemy. Daenerys is skeptical but Tyrion vouches for Jon. Jon says that they need to make cause to fight against the Army of the Dead.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/97/Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170829191511" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon meets Dany Queens Justice s7"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon meets Dany Queens Justice s7.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/97/Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170829191511"  	 width="180"  	 height="109"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/97/Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170829191511" 	 alt="Jon meets Dany Queens Justice s7"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon meets Dany Queens Justice s7.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="109"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_meets_Dany_Queens_Justice_s7.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Daenerys explains her self-faith to Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Daenerys asks Jon if his father knew that his friend King Robert had sent assassins to kill her as a baby; overlooking the fact that Lord <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a> had opposed King <a href="/wiki/Robert_Baratheon" title="Robert Baratheon">Robert Baratheon</a>'s assassination plot and Robert had rescinded said plot on his deathbed (though, she may be unaware of that). Dany recounts that she was targeted by assassins, enslaved, raped, and defiled but that her faith in herself rather the gods kept her going. Daenerys talks about the miracle of her dragons' hatching and the Dothraki crossing the <a href="/wiki/Narrow_Sea" title="Narrow Sea">Narrow Sea</a>. When Daenerys reiterates that she is destined to rule the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Kingdoms" title="Seven Kingdoms">Seven Kingdoms</a>, Jon retorts that she will be ruling over a graveyard.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170805224912" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="703 Daenerys Davos Jon"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg" 	data-image-name="703 Daenerys Davos Jon.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170805224912"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170805224912" 	 alt="703 Daenerys Davos Jon"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg" 	data-image-name="703 Daenerys Davos Jon.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:703_Daenerys_Davos_Jon.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon and Daenerys discuss his kingship.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Tyrion says they cannot split their forces. Davos then speaks up for his king and tells Dany that Jon won the support of the <a href="/wiki/Wildlings" title="Wildlings" class="mw-redirect">Wildlings</a> and fought the <a href="/wiki/White_Walkers" title="White Walkers">White Walkers</a>. Davos also mentions that Jon Snow came back from the dead. Davos says that it doesn't matter who bends the knee. Tyrion doesn't see the point of Jon Snow's refusal to submit. When Jon disputes Daenerys's claims to queenship, Dany responds that he is in open rebellion since he has declared himself King in the North. Daenerys then receives a message from <a href="/wiki/Varys" title="Varys">Varys</a>. Dany orders Missandei to give Jon and his followers food and lodging. When Jon asks if he is a prisoner, she says not yet.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/Jon_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731203316" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon TQJ"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon TQJ.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/Jon_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203316"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/9b/Jon_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203316" 	 alt="Jon TQJ"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon TQJ.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_TQJ.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon examines Dragonstone.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Jon and Tyrion discuss his predicament. Jon is unhappy that he is a prisoner while the White Walkers and the Night King still pose a threat. Tyrion says he trusts the word ofJeor Mormontand Jon. Jon asks Tyrion how he can convince people about the existence of things which they don't believe exist. Jon wants to help his people and is frustrated with the deadlock. Tyrion encourages Jon not to give up. When Jon remarks that he is a fool for going south, Tyrion reassures him that the Mad King's daughter is not her father and has protected people from "monsters," telling him to speak with her servants. Tyrion asks if there is something he can do to help Jon.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/45/Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170731203315" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon and Dany TQJ"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Dany TQJ.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/45/Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203315"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/45/Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170731203315" 	 alt="Jon and Dany TQJ"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon and Dany TQJ.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_and_Dany_TQJ.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dany allows Jon to mine for the Dragonglass.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Dany is watching over her dragons, she is joined by Jon. Dany tells Jon that she named her dragons <a href="/wiki/Rhaegal" title="Rhaegal">Rhaegal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Viserion" title="Viserion">Viserion</a> after her brothers <a href="/wiki/Rhaegar_Targaryen" title="Rhaegar Targaryen">Rhaegar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Viserys_Targaryen" title="Viserys Targaryen">Viserys Targaryen</a>. Jon realizes that Tyrion has been petitioning her. Dany tells Jon she is determined to remove Cersei. She allows Jon to mine the dragonglass and agrees to provide men and equipment. When he asks if she believes in the Night King and White Walkers, she tells him to get to work.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[57]</a></sup> Later, Jon leads Daenerys on a tour of the long-abandoned Valyrian dragonglass mine that Samwell Tarly told him about. The mine is ancient and impressive, used by the First Men long before the Valyrians came to Dragonstone. But this is not why Jon asked Daenerys to come.
</p><p>As they proceed deeper into the mines led by torchlight, Jon shows her cave paintings they discovered left behind by the Children of the Forest, filled with arcane magical symbols. Daenerys is stunned that the mythical Children stood where they are standing now, thousands upon thousands of years ago, long before mankind ever arrived in Westeros. Jon says this isn't exactly true, leading her into another chamber, this one filled with narrative drawings of the Children and the First Men. Daenerys wonders if the Children and First Men fought each other, but Jon then shows her ancient carvings of the White Walkers themselves, one of which Jon recognizes as an image of the Night King. Jon explains that the Children of the Forest and the First Men only managed to drive off the White Walkers the first time during the Long Night because they chose to join together to fight off their own extinction, and that is the choice between Jon and Daenerys now.
</p><p>Jon still wants Daenerys to ally with him to defeat the army of the dead. He insists that the North won't accept a southern ruler again after everything that has happened to them. Daenerys urges that they will if their king does. If his point in showing her the cave drawings was that she should swallow her pride and ally with him because the White Walkers are such a world-ending threat, by the same token, the North should submit to her, because their survival should outweigh their pride. When Daenerys receives word about Casterly Rock and Highgarden, she becomes frustrated about her constant defeat, and asks Jon whether if she must utilize her dragons in her conquest. Jon tells Daenerys that he never thought that it was impossible for dragons to live again, and that people follow Daenerys because she have done the impossible. He then warns her that if she uses her dragons to melt castles and burn cities, she will be just the same as those before her. Afterwards, Jon reunited with Theon who has survived his encounter with Euron. The anxious Theon asks Jon if Sansa is all right. Jon proceeds to scold Theon that what he did for Sansa was the only reason why he is still alive.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[58]</a></sup>
</p><p>Some time later, Jon witnesses Daenerys returning to Dragonstone on Drogon. Drogon approaches Jon who does not flinch at the dragon and starts to pet him, much to Daeneryss amazement. They then meet with Jorah Mormont who has returned from <a href="/wiki/Oldtown" title="Oldtown">Oldtown</a>. Jon then receives a letter regarding the army of the dead approaching <a href="/wiki/Eastwatch-by-the-Sea" title="Eastwatch-by-the-Sea">Eastwatch-by-the-Sea</a>. Tyrion proposes a plan to capture a wight to prove Cersei about the existence of the White Walkers. Jon agrees and departs with Davos, Jorah, and <a href="/wiki/Gendry" title="Gendry" class="mw-redirect">Gendry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E65_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E65-5">[6]</a></sup>
</p><p>Jon arrives at <a href="/wiki/Eastwatch-by-the-Sea" title="Eastwatch-by-the-Sea">Eastwatch-by-the-Sea</a> and heads out with a ranging party consisting of <a href="/wiki/Tormund" title="Tormund">Tormund</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jorah_Mormont" title="Jorah Mormont">Jorah Mormont</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gendry" title="Gendry" class="mw-redirect">Gendry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sandor_Clegane" title="Sandor Clegane">Sandor Clegane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thoros" title="Thoros">Thoros</a>, <a href="/wiki/Beric_Dondarrion" title="Beric Dondarrion">Beric Dondarrion</a>, and a few others on a <a href="/wiki/Wight_Hunt" title="Wight Hunt">mission</a> to capture a wight. They succeed but half of the party, including Thoros, end up being killed as they are attacked by wights, prompting Daenerys to intervene with all three of her dragons and leading to the death of Viserion by the Night King, who later resurrects the beast for his own use. Despite this devastating loss, Jon continues to fight and nearly drowns in the cold waters beneath the ice. Though he manages to pull himself out, he is all alone and nearly overwhelmed by the wights until a last-minute intervention by his long-lost uncle Benjen, who tells him to flee on his horse while he buys time for his nephew to escape. While riding away on horseback, Jon watches his uncle being overwhelmed by the undead. He makes it back to Eastwatch and is brought aboard the ship with Dany, Davos, and Sandor.
</p><p>In the Narrow Sea, Jon Snow wakes to find Daenerys watching over him in his chambers. Jon apologizes for the disastrous ranging party and the fact it caused Viserion's death, but Daenerys tells him not to apologize because she now knows that the Army of the Dead is real. Overcome with emotion, she tells Jon that the dragons are the only children she will ever have, and vows that she and Jon will together destroy the Night King. Jon thanks her for her support, addressing her as "Dany", and Daenerys realizes that the last person to address her by that name was her older brother (and Jon's uncle) Viserys Targaryen, who Daenerys remembers as not being a good person. Jon apologizes and asks if "My Queen" would be more appropriate; realizing he is agreeing to bend the knee (though both of them are still unaware that <i>he</i> is the rightful heir to the Iron Throne), Daenerys asks Jon what the Northern lords loyal to him will make of this. Jon assures her they will come to see her for the good person she is, as he already has. Touched by his statement, Daenerys gently takes Jon's hand in her own for a moment. They gaze into each other's eye for a moment  a long moment  but Daenerys suddenly pulls away and tells him to get some rest and leaves him alone.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[59]</a></sup>
</p><p>After recovering from his ordeal, Jon and the rest of his allies head to the <a href="/wiki/Dragonpit" title="Dragonpit">Dragonpit</a> to <a href="/wiki/Parley_in_King%27s_Landing" title="Parley in King's Landing" class="mw-redirect">parley</a> with the Lannisters. When Cersei dismisses their warnings about the Night King and his army as a ploy to trick her into lowering her defenses, they rattle the <a href="/wiki/Captured_wight" title="Captured wight">captured wight</a> into lunging for her, making her and her allies see once and for all that the threat from <a href="/wiki/Beyond_the_Wall" title="Beyond the Wall">beyond the Wall</a> is real. Jon steps forward and picks up the wight's discarded hand, using a torch provided by Davos to demonstrate how fire can be used to stop them. He then uses a dragonglass dagger to the heart to end the wight's upper half, bluntly stating that if they don't win the coming war, such a fate awaits every person in Westeros. Seemingly convinced, Cersei immediately offers terms: satisfied that Daenerys is concerned with the Army of the Dead, Cersei will not withdraw her troops, but will guarantee that they will not hinder the Targaryen or Northern forces in any way during the battle against the White Walkers. She refuses to deal with Daenerys at all, however, and calls on Jon Snow, as King in the North and Ned Stark's son, to keep the truce and to stay out of any future conflict between Cersei and Daenerys. Jon, however, says that he cannot serve two queens - and reveals to all assembled that he has already declared for Daenerys, infuriating all three Lannisters present. Declaring that there will be no truce if it is just her and Daenerys, Cersei storms out, content to let the Starks and Targaryens battle the undead alone and then deal with whoever emerges victorious from that conflict.
</p><p>Daenerys and Tyrion rip into Jon over his ill-advised action, suggesting that learning to lie just a little might be a good skill. Jon responds by arguing that while such an attitude may or may not have contributed to getting his father killed, if no one is willing to speak the truth, then everyone's word is worthless, and lies will not help them win the coming fight. While Tyrion goes to talk to Cersei, Daenerys and Jon discuss the dragons and how her ancestors caged them, and in turn, become less impressive as the power of the dragons waned. Jon questions Daenerys's assertion of infertility, particularly when she admits that she never got an informed opinion about her condition from anyone except Mirri Maz Duur herself. Their conversation is interrupted by the return of all three Lannisters. Cersei has agreed to work with Daenerys, but not by keeping her troops back: the Lannister army will march north to fight alongside the Starks and Targaryens. Little do Jon and Daenerys know that Cersei has no intention of keeping her promise and that she intends to let them fight the White Walkers on their own and mop up whoever wins with the help of the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Company" title="Golden Company">Golden Company</a>. Jaime refuses to back down from his pledge to help fight the White Walkers and defies his sister-lover by traveling north. Whether he will warn Jon and Daenerys of Cersei's plan remains to be seen.
</p><p>Later, as the two of them ride a ship to White Harbor, Jon enters Daenerys's cabin where the two of them begin to consummate their relationship, still unaware that they are aunt and nephew.
</p><p>Meanwhile, back at Winterfell, Samwell Tarly and Gilly arrive. The former visits Bran and the two of them discuss Jon's origin: he was born to Rhaegar Targaryen and Lyanna Stark at a Tower in Dorne, and is not a Snow at all, but a Sand. Sam realizes that that isn't true either, recalling the entry from High Septon Maynard's private journal about annulling Rhaegar's marriage. Bran expressed his doubts, but Sam reiterates the private nature of the journal and encourages Bran to use Greensight to confirm it. To his own surprise, Bran easily finds the wedding, where he sees a clearly happy Lyanna wedding Rhaegar in a Faith of the Seven ceremony before a Heart tree. Warging forward to the Tower of Joy, Bran finally hears Lyanna's dying words. Now piecing the truth together, Bran declares that Rhaegar never raped Lyanna. She loved him and ran off with him, and bore him a son, Aegon Targaryen, making "Jon" not only legitimate but the rightful heir to the Iron Throne.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[60]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Season_8"><a href="/wiki/Season_8" title="Season 8">Season 8</a></span></h3>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190415233146" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Dany Jon March to Winterfell Ep"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dany Jon March to Winterfell Ep.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190415233146"  	 width="180"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/9/98/Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190415233146" 	 alt="Dany Jon March to Winterfell Ep"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dany Jon March to Winterfell Ep.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="103"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dany_Jon_March_to_Winterfell_Ep.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon returns to Winterfell with the Targaryen forces.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Upon arrival in the North, Jon and Daenerys, along with their combined forces, march through <a href="/wiki/Winter_town" title="Winter town">Winter town</a> on their way to Winterfell. The townspeople cast Daenerys many suspicious looks, and Jon reminds her that Northerners have a long-established distrust of outsiders. Upon arriving at Winterfell, he introduces her to Sansa. Jon and Daenerys later ride Daenerys's dragons, Jon riding Rhaegal and Daenerys riding Drogon. They find a waterfall where Jon used to hunt as a child and they share an intimate moment.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8f/Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190415031706" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Dragon Riding S8 Ep 1"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dragon Riding S8 Ep 1.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8f/Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190415031706"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/8/8f/Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190415031706" 	 alt="Dragon Riding S8 Ep 1"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg" 	data-image-name="Dragon Riding S8 Ep 1.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dragon_Riding_S8_Ep_1.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon rides Rhaegal for the first time.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later, Jon meets up with Sansa, who is angry that Jon bent the knee to Daenerys. Jon says titles are not important when the Army of the Dead is coming and he is certain Daenerys will make a good queen for them. Sansa asks Jon if he bent the knee to save the North or because he loves Daenerys, who later invites him to ride atop <a href="/wiki/Rhaegal" title="Rhaegal">Rhaegal</a>. While he initially finds it difficult, he soon gets used to it. After landing, he and Daenerys share a kiss which leaves both the dragons jealous and intimidated. When he reunites with Arya, he finds out that she is more loyal to Sansa than the Targaryen queen.<sup id="cite_ref-E68_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E68-60">[61]</a></sup>
</p><p>Later in the catacombs when he is lighting candles in remembrance of his family, Jon reunites with <a href="/wiki/Samwell_Tarly" title="Samwell Tarly">Sam</a>. Sam asks him whether he knew about Daenerys burning <a href="/wiki/Dickon_Tarly" title="Dickon Tarly">his brother</a> and <a href="/wiki/Randyll_Tarly" title="Randyll Tarly">father</a>, but Jon is surprised. Sam tells him he'll make a better king and reveals his true parentage to him, he is Aegon - the son of <a href="/wiki/Rhaegar_Targaryen" title="Rhaegar Targaryen">Rhaegar Targaryen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lyanna_Stark" title="Lyanna Stark">Lyanna Stark</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-E68_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E68-60">[61]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c1/Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190417203101" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Arya S8 EP2"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Arya S8 EP2.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c1/Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190417203101"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c1/Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190417203101" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Arya S8 EP2"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Arya S8 EP2.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_%26_Arya_S8_EP2.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon plans the defense of Winterfell.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Stark and Targaryen forces prepare to fight the dead near Winterfell. Bran offers himself as bait to lure the <a href="/wiki/Night_King" title="Night King">Night King</a> for an ambush in the <a href="/wiki/Godswood" title="Godswood">Godswood</a> of Winterfell. Jon opts to use the dragons to protect Bran in the Godswood. Later, Jon informs Daenerys about his true parentage in the crypts. Daenerys is distrustful and claims it is convenient that only Bran and Sam know of this. They are interrupted by sounds of horns which signal the arrival of the Night King's army.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[62]</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Winterfell_(Great_War)" title="Battle of Winterfell (Great War)">Battle of Winterfell</a>, Jon rides atop Rhaegal and leads him in fighting the dead. He and <a href="/wiki/Drogon" title="Drogon">Drogon</a> battle the Night King and the undead <a href="/wiki/Viserion" title="Viserion">Viserion</a> with Rhaegal being heavily injured. Rhaegal is able to land on the ground but falls unconscious due to his injuries while landing and Jon is knocked off from the dragon's top. He is wounded during the battle and is pinned down by Viserion, though he survives as the Night King's army is obliterated with his death.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[63]</a></sup>
</p><p>After the battle, Jon leads a mass cremation for the dead and is hailed by the wildlings during the celebrations of the victory. After the celebrations, Daenerys meets up with Jon in his room. Jon offers his condolences for Jorah's death and Daenerys affirms that Jorah loved her but she couldn't love him the way he wanted, not the way she loves Jon. She and Jon begin to kiss, preparing to have sex but Jon stops himself. Daenerys laments that Jon told her the truth of his parentage and is fearful people will press his claim against hers for the Iron Throne. Jon is vehement that he does not want the throne. Daenerys tells Jon it doesn't matter what he personally wants, people will press his claim. Jon tells Daenerys he will refuse and on his knee, declares Daenerys will always be his queen. Daenerys insists that he must never reveal his parentage to anyone but Jon tells Daenerys he owes his sisters the truth. He is certain they can all live happily together but Daenerys says the only way that can happen is if Jon never tells the truth about himself and leaves.<sup id="cite_ref-E71_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E71-63">[64]</a></sup>
</p><p>While making the plans for attacking <a href="/wiki/King%27s_Landing" title="King's Landing">King's Landing</a>, Daenerys wants to take the Red Keep while Tyrion and Jon vouch for a siege in hopes this will reduce casualties. Sansa opts for letting their forces rest before charging into another battle. Jon, however, assures the queen that they will obey her command. Afterward, Sansa and Arya state that they do not trust her. When Jon defends Daenerys and says that they only have to get to know her, Sansa and Arya reply they never will as she is not one of them. Jon says he has never been a Stark but they both insist he is. Pained, Jon looks at Bran, who says that it's his choice to tell them. Jon makes them both swear to never tell anyone the secret he is about to reveal to them. After they do, then at a loss for words, Jon tells Bran to reveal the truth of his parentage to them.<sup id="cite_ref-E71_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E71-63">[64]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190513025908" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Varys S8 Ep5"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Varys S8 Ep5.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513025908"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/f/fb/Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513025908" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Varys S8 Ep5"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Varys S8 Ep5.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_%26_Varys_S8_Ep5.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Varys discusses the Iron Throne with Jon.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon marches to King's Landing along the <a href="/wiki/Kingsroad" title="Kingsroad">Kingsroad</a> with the surviving Stark, Arryn, and <a href="/wiki/Dothraki" title="Dothraki">Dothraki</a> forces unopposed while the <a href="/wiki/Unsullied" title="Unsullied">Unsullied</a> reach the capital ahead of them. Hopes for a peaceful surrender, however, are quickly extinguished with <a href="/wiki/Missandei" title="Missandei">Missandei</a>'s execution.<sup id="cite_ref-E71_63-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E71-63">[64]</a></sup> Later, Jon separates from his forces after crossing <a href="/wiki/The_Trident" title="The Trident">the Trident</a> and heads back to <a href="/wiki/Dragonstone" title="Dragonstone" class="mw-redirect">Dragonstone</a>. Varys informs him about Daenerys' unstable state of mind and is requested by him to take the <a href="/wiki/Iron_Throne" title="Iron Throne">Iron Throne</a>, but he refuses.
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0b/Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190513025907" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Dany S8 Ep5"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Dany S8 Ep5.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0b/Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513025907"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/0/0b/Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513025907" 	 alt="Jon &amp;amp; Dany S8 Ep5"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg" 	data-image-name="Jon &amp;amp; Dany S8 Ep5.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jon_%26_Dany_S8_Ep5.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon discusses his parentage with Daenerys.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Daenerys later has Varys executed for treason. When Varys is burned alive by Drogon's flames, Jon is disturbed by the execution via fire. Later, Jon comes to see Daenerys and she blames Jon telling Sansa about her parentage for what happened. Jon states he doesn't want the crown which is what he told Varys, with Daenerys replying Sansa betrayed his trust and is as responsible for Varys' death as she is. Daenerys confides that the people of <a href="/wiki/Westeros" title="Westeros">Westeros</a> love Jon more than her, that all she has here is fear, not love. Jon tells Daenerys that he loves her and she will always be his queen. As she asks if that's all she is to him, the two kiss but Jon breaks it off, still hesitant over their blood ties. Daenerys accepts this but resigns herself to ruling by fear.<sup id="cite_ref-E72_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E72-64">[65]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/STARKENTOURAGEBE%3B%3BS.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20190513044715" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="STARKENTOURAGEBE;;S"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="STARKENTOURAGEBE%3B%3BS.jpeg" 	data-image-name="STARKENTOURAGEBE;;S.jpeg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/STARKENTOURAGEBE%3B%3BS.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513044715"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/c8/STARKENTOURAGEBE%3B%3BS.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190513044715" 	 alt="STARKENTOURAGEBE;;S"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="STARKENTOURAGEBE%3B%3BS.jpeg" 	data-image-name="STARKENTOURAGEBE;;S.jpeg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:STARKENTOURAGEBE;;S.jpeg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon leads his forces into King's Landing.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Battle of King's Landing">Battle of King's Landing</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Company" title="Golden Company">Golden Company</a> is caught off-guard by Drogon and as a result, is decimated by the charging Northern and Targaryen forces. The surviving Lannister forces surrender but Daenerys refuses to accept. Both the Targaryen and Northern forces start slaughtering the unarmed Lannister forces as Jon tries in vain to hold them back. As a result, the Lannisters who havesurrendered start clashing again, and Jon is forced to fight to deflect their attacks. He is horrified by the carnage that occurs despite his calls to stop it, and kills one of his soldiers trying to rape a woman. When the <a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">wildfire</a> caches <a href="/wiki/Wildfire_Plot" title="Wildfire Plot">stored below the city years ago</a> by <a href="/wiki/Aerys_II_Targaryen" title="Aerys II Targaryen">Aerys II Targaryen</a> start erupting due to Drogon's dragonfire, Jon orders his forces to evacuate.<sup id="cite_ref-E72_64-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E72-64">[65]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cb/Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190520025951" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Worm Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg" 	data-image-name="Worm Jon S8 Ep6.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cb/Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520025951"  	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cb/Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520025951" 	 alt="Worm Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg" 	data-image-name="Worm Jon S8 Ep6.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="120"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Worm_Jon_S8_Ep6.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon confronts Grey Worm over executing surrendered Lannister soldiers.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the battle, Jon, Davos, and Tyrion observein horror the ash-covered devastationwrought by Daenerys, with charred bodies strewn everywhere. Tyrion leaves for the <a href="/wiki/Red_Keep" title="Red Keep">Red Keep</a> alone and rejects Jon's suggestions to take some of his soldiers as guards. A little while later, Jon confronts <a href="/wiki/Grey_Worm" title="Grey Worm">Grey Worm</a> and the Unsullied who are executing captive Lannister soldiers. Grey Worm states that he has been ordered by Daenerys to execute all who followed Cersei. When Jon tries to stop him, the Unsullied and Stark soldiers almost come to blows, but Davos defuses the situation by telling Jon to take it up with the queen. As they walk away, they witness Grey Worm executing the captives.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/10/Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest?cb=20190530024651" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Arya warns Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" 	data-image-name="Arya warns Jon S8 Ep6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/10/Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190530024651"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/1/10/Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190530024651" 	 alt="Arya warns Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" 	data-image-name="Arya warns Jon S8 Ep6.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Arya_warns_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Arya warns Jon against Daenerys.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At the Red Keep, Jon witnesses Daenerys giving a speech to her victorious forces and Tyrion disavowing his loyalty and being arrested for releasing Jaime. He then reunites with an injured Arya. Surprised, he asks why she was in King's Landing, to which Arya responds that she came to kill Cersei, but Daenerys got there first. She warns Jon that he will always be a danger to her because of his parentage and Sansa will never bend the knee to her.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/33/Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest?cb=20190530030420" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Tyrion pleads Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" 	data-image-name="Tyrion pleads Jon S8 Ep6.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/33/Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190530030420"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/33/Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190530030420" 	 alt="Tyrion pleads Jon S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" 	data-image-name="Tyrion pleads Jon S8 Ep6.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tyrion_pleads_Jon_S8_Ep6.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Tyrion pleads with Jon to take action against Daenerys.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A while later, Jon visits the imprisoned Tyrion, who expects he'll be executed soon. Tyrion admits that Varys was right all along about Daenerys. He warns Jon that she won't stop until she has "liberated" the world and rules it all. He recounts her atrocities but Jon states it happened because of the trauma from the loss of loved ones she suffered. Tyrion states he knows Jon doesn't want to betray her and knows Jon loves her, he loved her too. He admits he is asking Jon to do a terrible thing but advises him to take action because she is now the greatest threat to the people. He warns that he'll always be in danger because of his parentage and asks if his sisters will ever bend the knee. Jon responds they'll always be loyal, but Tyrion reasons that Sansa told him about his parentage because she doesn't want Daenerys as the Queen. Jon responds that she can't choose, but Tyrion states he can and has to do it now.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ed/Queen_slayer.png/revision/latest?cb=20190520171423" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Queen slayer"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Queen_slayer.png" 	data-image-name="Queen slayer.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ed/Queen_slayer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520171423"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/e/ed/Queen_slayer.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520171423" 	 alt="Queen slayer"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Queen_slayer.png" 	data-image-name="Queen slayer.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Queen_slayer.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon holds Daenerys after assassinating her.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Troubled, Jon walks to the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> and finds Daenerys standing by the Iron Throne. Jon confronts her about her atrocities during the battle. She displays no remorse, believing it was necessary to achieve her ends. Jon tries to dissuade her from this path, urging forgiveness for Tyrion and those in King's Landing, which she rejects and states the world they need can't be built by those loyal to the current one. She assures that the new world she has in mind will be a good one. When Jon asks about others wanting to choose what is good, she responds they don't get to. She tries to convince him to be by her side to build her new world and an anguished Jon reaffirms his allegiance to her. As they share a passionate kiss, Jon reluctantly stabs her. Daenerys collapses and dies in his arms as Jon grieves over her. Drogon approaches them after witnessing this while Jon gently lays her on the ground. Seeing his mother dead on the floor, Drogon becomes enraged and faces Jon. Jon prepares for his death, but the dragon instead melts the <a href="/wiki/Iron_Throne" title="Iron Throne">Iron Throne</a> and flies away with her corpse, which Jon witnesses.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/30/John-in-jail.png/revision/latest?cb=20190520105432" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="John-in-jail"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="John-in-jail.png" 	data-image-name="John-in-jail.png" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/30/John-in-jail.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520105432"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/3/30/John-in-jail.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520105432" 	 alt="John-in-jail"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="John-in-jail.png" 	data-image-name="John-in-jail.png" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:John-in-jail.png" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon converses with Tyrion while being held as a prisoner.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Jon is imprisoned in the Red Keep for the murder of Daenerys. Despite being supposed to be <a href="/wiki/Great_Council_of_305_AC" title="Great Council of 305 AC">put on trial in front of the lords and ladies of Westeros</a>, he is absent because the Unsullied want to punish him themselves. Tyrion convinces Grey Worm to allow the new <a href="/wiki/King_of_the_Andals_and_the_First_Men" title="King of the Andals and the First Men" class="mw-redirect">King of the Andals and the First Men</a> punish him since the crime was committed in Westeros. Ultimately, Bran is elected as the king and decides to exile Jon to the Night's Watch in order to avoid a war between his supporters and the Unsullied. The new Hand of the King, Tyrion, later visits a defeated Jon and informs him of his fate. Jon dryly asks if there still is a Night's Watch, and Tyrion responds the world still needs a refuge for bastards and broken men. Jon states that he doesn't feel right about what he did, but Tyrion responds they did it together and to ask him in 10 years if it was right. Jon bids farewell to him, but Tyrion responds he might want to piss off the top of the Wall after serving a few years as the Hand.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cd/Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190520171747" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="Stark Sibling&amp;#039;s S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg" 	data-image-name="Stark Sibling&#39;s S8 Ep6.jpg" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cd/Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520171747"  	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/c/cd/Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190520171747" 	 alt="Stark Sibling&amp;#039;s S8 Ep6"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg" 	data-image-name="Stark Sibling&#39;s S8 Ep6.jpg" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="101"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Stark_Sibling%27s_S8_Ep6.jpg" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon bids farewell to his family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While being taken into exile by two <a href="/wiki/Wandering_crows" title="Wandering crows">wandering crows</a>, Jon bids farewell to Bran, Sansa, and Arya at the docks. Jon congratulates Sansa on gaining <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_North" title="Kingdom of the North">independence</a> for the North and assures her she will be a good leader when she laments they lost their king before they hug.Jon then tells Arya that she could to visit him at Castle Black, butArya states that she isn't going back North and plans to explore the uncharted seas to the west of Westeros before the two tearfully hug.Finally, Jonkneels before the new king Bran and apologizes for not being there when he needed him, but Bran states he was "exactly where he was supposed to be".<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="article-thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20190605164840" 	class="image image-thumbnail" 	 	 	><img src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" 	 alt="ExodusBeyondtheWall"  	class="thumbimage lzy lzyPlcHld " 	 	data-image-key="ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG" 	data-image-name="ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG" 	 data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190605164840"  	 width="180"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 onload="if(typeof ImgLzy===&#39;object&#39;){ImgLzy.load(this)}"  	><noscript><img src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/gameofthrones/images/4/4b/ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190605164840" 	 alt="ExodusBeyondtheWall"  	class="thumbimage " 	 	data-image-key="ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG" 	data-image-name="ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG" 	 	 width="180"  	 height="98"  	 	 	 	></noscript></a>  	<figcaption> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:ExodusBeyondtheWall.PNG" class="sprite info-icon"></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Jon rides north of the Wall, acommpanied by Tormund and the wildlings.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Some time later, Jon arrives at Castle Black and reunites with Tormund and the wildlings. Later, he dons the black cloak of a sworn brother of the Night's Watch and reunites with Ghost. He then leaves with Ghost and the wildlings for lands north of the Wall, watching forlornly as the gate to Castle Black closes behind him, and then rides into the <a href="/wiki/Haunted_Forest" title="Haunted Forest">Haunted Forest</a> alongside them.<sup id="cite_ref-E73_65-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-E73-65">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:The Kingsroad">"<i>You are a Stark. You may not have <a href="/wiki/House_Stark" title="House Stark">my name</a>, but you have my blood.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8213;<a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">Eddard Stark</a> to Jon before he leaves for the <a href="/wiki/Night%27s_Watch" title="Night's Watch">Night's Watch</a>.<span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/The_Kingsroad" title="The Kingsroad">[src]</a></sup></span></div>Because he was raised by Ned Stark at Winterfell, Jon has adopted a clear moral compass and a true sense of honor, which he tries his hardest to abide by even when he must make a difficult decision, especially after he became Lord Commander of the Night's Watch. He has always admired and idolized his father, but due to Catelyn Stark's cold disdain for Jon, Eddard was careful not to give him more attention than his lawful children by Catelyn. Lady Stark was never actively mean to Jon, but because he wasn't her own son she intentionally ignored him (as is common for bastard children), meaning that Jon grew up without a mother-figure. Nor did Jon consider Catelyn's behavior to be unusual or unexpected: it is rare for a noble to raise their bastard child alongside their lawful children, and his presence was a great insult to her honor.
</dd></dl>
<p>While his interactions with Catelyn remained awkward or nonexistent, he actually became good friends with his half-siblings, particularly Robb and Arya. Robb was of the same age as Jon so they became playmates and comrades in training, while due to her tomboyish personality Arya was also something of a social misfit like Jon, which they bonded over. His closeness with Brandon and Rickon was proved when the latter had to leave Winterfell and Master Luwin advised them to go, Castle Black, where the old man was sure that their half-brother would keep them safe. With Sansa on the other hand, according to the talk they had when they reunited at Castle Black, the friendship has never been deep as those between Jon and the other siblings. Since then, however, Sansa proves to have great faith in her half-brother by standing up for him when he is King in the North and, when she discovers his true parentage, by seeing him as the best candidate to become King of the Seven Kingdoms. Also, when Jon is forced to join again the Night's Watch, Sansa shows great sorrow and thinks that sending Jon away is both a great unfairness and a great loss for the North.
</p><p>Like many bastard children, Jon had to learn to grow up quickly. This made Jon mature and perceptive beyond his age, so he could navigate his complicated relationships within the Stark household. His bastard status has also made Jon something of a loner, solemn and somber with a desire to prove himself to society and to his father. Jon thought that the best way for a bastard in his position to gain honor and respect was to join the Night's Watch, emulating his uncle Benjen, because past social status is ignored after joining the Watch. Despite his introverted demeanor, Jon is very compassionate and protective of his fellow outcasts such as Samwell Tarly, Grenn, and Pyp.
</p><p>In many ways, Jon has been unusually lucky for a bastard child, given how rare it is for a lord to raise one in his own castle alongside his lawful children. For all of Jon's misgivings about not knowing his mother and Catelyn ignoring and shunning him, he was loved by his father and siblings, was never poor or hungry, but lived in a castle and had a noble's upbringing. Jon was formally educated by Maester Luwin and was trained in combat by Ser Rodrik Cassel, excelling at swordsmanship. This made Jon somewhat arrogant when he was a new recruit at Castle Black until Tyrion pointed out that the other recruits were all far less fortunate than he was. This humbles Jon, and he changes his behavior to be the champion of the other downtrodden recruits and helps train them by walking them through the swordplay techniques he knows.
</p><p>The Starks were an interfaith household, with Eddard and Catelyn's children being exposed to not only the religion of the Old Gods of the Forest worshiped by most Northmen, but also Catelyn's devout adherence to the Faith of the Seven. Because Jon had no real interaction with Catelyn and revered his father Eddard, he was not exposed to the Seven but proudly keeps to the Old Gods, and honors the traditions of his <a href="/wiki/First_Men" title="First Men">First Men</a> ancestors. When Jon took his vow to become a member of the Night's Watch, he chose to do so in front of a heart tree, sacred to the Old Gods.
</p><p>Jon is also fairly shy around women, and as he revealed to Samwell, he was a virgin when he joined the Night's Watch. While he was attractive enough, as a bastard son with nothing to inherit he had no realistic marriage prospects with noblewomen. Jon was even wary of having sex with random girls or prostitutes (as Theon did) because he was terrified of fathering a bastard of his own: having lived his life as a bastard, he felt that it wasn't a life another child should have to go through.
</p><p>However, death has changed Jon. Despite his honorable convictions and previous commitment to the Night's Watch, his experience of being murdered by his own men and then revived has made Jon somewhat more cynical and nihilistic. No longer believing in himself and his ability to face the coming threat, due to being murdered for doing what he thought was right - Jon abandons the Night's Watch, despite knowing full well how dangerous the threat looming beyond the Wall really is. He loses his determination about fighting and becomes much more lonely and melancholic only speaking when he hasn't any other choice. Also, Jon feels remorse for hanging his former steward Olly, even though the latter did murder both him and the woman he loved. While he is wary of conflict since his return, his love for his family has brought him back into the fight. To this end, Jon chooses his family over the Night's Watch - a choice he once attempted to make when Robb marched off to war but forsook in the past. When Ramsay decides to play a "game" with Rickon, Jon once again chooses his family by attempting to save his little brother's life, even at the cost of his own life and battle plans.
</p><p>The revelation that he is a Targaryen has made no difference to Jon; he has remainedloyal to his origins, as a Northman and a Stark, and through much suffering, many hard choices and also some mistakes, Jon proved to be a born leader. To protect his land and family, in just a few years he has risen up from being a bastard to becoming the King in the North, a prominent figure among the Free Folks and the one who many have acknowledged as the most suitable to become King of the Seven Kingdoms.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships"> Relationships </span></h2>
<p><i>Main: <a href="/wiki/Jon_Snow_and_Ygritte" title="Jon Snow and Ygritte">Jon Snow and Ygritte</a></i>
</p>
<ul><li> <a href="/wiki/Ygritte" title="Ygritte">Ygritte</a>: She was Jon's first love, although in their first encounter she tries to seduce and cheat him. When Jon infiltrates the Wildlings, they become lovers and Jon really falls in love with her, but ultimately he chooses his vows for the Night's Watch over her. Ygritte shoots him with three arrows but due to her feelings for Jon, she couldn't bring herself to kill him. In the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Castle_Black" title="Battle of Castle Black">Battle of Castle Black</a>, Ygritte was killed by Olly and died in Jon's arms. A devastated Jon cremates her body just beyond the Wall, per Tormund's suggestion that she belongs in the true North.
</li></ul>
<p><i>Main: <a href="/wiki/Jon_Snow_and_Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Jon Snow and Daenerys Targaryen">Jon Snow and Daenerys Targaryen</a> </i>
</p>
<ul><li> <a href="/wiki/Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Daenerys Targaryen">Daenerys Targaryen</a>: She was the Mad King's daughter and the youngest sister of Jon's father, Prince Rhaegar, making her his aunt by blood. Having been summoned from Winterfell to bend the knee to Daenerys, Jon initially refuses on the grounds that they need to ally against the Night King and the army of the dead instead of removing Cersei from the Iron Throne. After witnessing the large numbers of the army of the dead, Daenerys agrees to help Jon and during their time together, they fall in love. They fight the Army of the Dead in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Winterfell_(Great_War)" title="Battle of Winterfell (Great War)">Battle of Winterfell</a>, during which the Night King is defeated. With the Long Night prevented, Jon honors his pledge to help Daenerys take the Iron Throne. However, she <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_King%27s_Landing" title="Battle of King's Landing">razes King's Landing</a> after the city surrenders, killing thousands of civilians. Unable to dissuade her from continuing this destruction, Jon reluctantly <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Daenerys_Targaryen" title="Assassination of Daenerys Targaryen">assassinates Daenerys</a>, and she dies in his arms as he grieves.
</li></ul>

My <a href="/wiki/Eddard_Stark" title="Eddard Stark">father</a> wouldn't even tell me her name. I don't know if she's living or dead. I don't know if she's a noblewoman or a fisherman's wife or a whore...</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8213;Jon Snow to <a href="/wiki/Samwell_Tarly" title="Samwell Tarly">Samwell Tarly</a><span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/Cripples,_Bastards,_and_Broken_Things" title="Cripples, Bastards, and Broken Things">[src]</a></sup></span></div>

<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:Hardhome (episode)">"<i>I'm not asking <a href="/wiki/Karsi" title="Karsi">you</a> to forget your dead. Ill never forget mine. I lost fifty brothers the night that <a href="/wiki/Mance_Rayder" title="Mance Rayder">Mance</a> <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Castle_Black" title="Battle of Castle Black">attacked</a> the Wall. But Im asking you to think about your children now. Theyll never have children of their own if we dont band together. The <a href="/wiki/Long_Night" title="Long Night">Long Night</a> is coming and the <a href="/wiki/Wights" title="Wights">dead</a> come with it. No clan can stop them. The <a href="/wiki/Free_Folk" title="Free Folk">Free Folk</a> cant stop them, the <a href="/wiki/Night%E2%80%99s_Watch" title="Nights Watch" class="mw-redirect">Nights Watch</a> cant stop them and all the southern kings cant stop them! Only together. All of us. And even then it may not be enough, but at least we give the <a href="/wiki/White_Walkers" title="White Walkers">fuckers</a> a fight.</i>"</span>
</dd><dd>&#8213;Jon Snow<span class="noprint"><sup><a href="/wiki/Hardhome_(episode)" title="Hardhome (episode)">[src]</a></sup></span></div>
</dd></dl>
